Chairman Han, upon the order of the Central Government, is receiving the troops, designating Gaotang and Linyi counties as their garrison area. This morning, about five or six hundred of Shi's cavalry brigade arrived in Dezhou and are currently stationed at Qilipu, south of the city. Tonight, five or six thousand of its special service brigade will also arrive in Dezhou. After a short rest, they will all be sent to the designated area to await roll call and reorganization. Shi's troops have lost all their artillery in this battle. The Mi Wenhe and Sun Guangqian troops have been cut into several sections, and their whereabouts are currently unknown.

Cao Fulin, the commander of the 29th Division, arrived in Dezhou from Yucheng on the 4th to handle the reception of Shi's troops. He is currently stationed on an armored train at the station. The troops stationed in Dezhou are the first regiment of Li Hanzhang's troops of the 85th Brigade of the 29th Division, the first regiment of Sun's troops of the 24th Brigade, and one regiment of Zhao Xinde's brigade. The local area is as peaceful as ever. (5th)

Suppressing the Red Army Captures Xingguo 48

Besieged for Several Days, Killing Countless Bandits

The Remaining Bandits Were All Captured and Disarmed

Nanchang Communication: Xingguo is located south of Donggu, bordering Ningdu to the east, Yudu and Ganxian to the south, Taihe and Wan'an along the Gan River to the west, and Yongfeng and Ji'an to the north. The depth of banditry there is even greater than in Ningdu and Ji'an. It was originally one of the Red Bandit bases. Last year, when the 19th Route Army entered Jiangxi from Hunan, after capturing Lianhua, Yongxin, Wan'an, and Suichuan counties and stationing in Ganzhou, Yudu and Xingguo were also recovered by the army one after another. Various bandit nests in Xing territory, such as Jiangbei Cave, were destroyed by Cai's division. However, due to the defeat of Zhang Huizan's division, the army was ordered to reinforce Ji'an. When the Jiang and Cai divisions marched east from Ganzhou to Ji'an, no less than ten thousand civilians from Yu and Xing fled with the army. The army marched in the morning, and Xing and Yu fell to the bandits in the evening. After the Suppression Army recaptured Ningdu and Donggu this time, Zhu, Mao, Peng, Huang, and other remnants all fled to Yudu and Xingguo counties. The Suppression Army took advantage of the victory to continue the suppression. The bandit nests bordering Ningdu, Yudu, and Donggu, such as Gulonggang, Jinyizhai, Chenggang, and Liantang, were all captured one after another. Then, they surrounded Xingguo County. However, most of the bandits recently attempted to flee west again. Only two or three thousand bandits remained in the city, but they still stubbornly resisted. The Suppression Army then launched a fierce attack on the county seat. The air force stationed in Ji'an flew to the county seat every day to drop bombs. At the same time, the Suppression Army also used machine guns and artillery to fiercely bombard the bandit troops defending the city. Many bandits were killed and wounded. The remaining bandits could no longer hold on. The Suppression Army then captured Xingcheng at around 4 PM on the afternoon of the 4th. The bandits in the city could not escape and were all captured and disarmed. Various puppet agencies were also destroyed. According to the victory telegram sent by Zhao Guantao, roughly stating that tens of thousands of bandits in Xingguo were besieged by our various units for several days, killing countless bandits. Our 32nd Regiment first captured the county seat at 4 PM on the Zhi day. The remaining bandits were all captured and are currently being disarmed, etc. Since the 16th year of the Republic of China to the present, the bandits have occupied Xingguo most of the time. Therefore, families of the middle and upper classes have long since fled. The lower classes of society and local ruffians have formed a pact with the Red Bandits, plundering wantonly. Puppet Soviet governments have been established everywhere. All fields and houses have been confiscated. Now, not only are the fields desolate and the houses in ruins, but the boundaries of the entire county's fields have been leveled and cannot be distinguished. Those who have fled to Ganzhou and the provincial capital are still in exile. The disaster relief and reconstruction in the future will not be easy. (August 5th)

He Jian Telegram Reports

News of the Guangxi Army Invading Hunan 49

Nanchang Communication: According to the war zone headquarters bulletin, He Jian telegraphed that the Guangxi rebel Tan Yuanfang's troops have arrived at Shazipu and Taiyanpu in Quanzhou. Another part arrived at Huangsha River on the winter evening, and the bulk of Li Pinxian's forces will continue to advance towards Quanzhou and will soon be stationed in Yongzhou (Lingling) to join forces with Heng (Zhou) Bao (Qing). Furthermore, according to reconnaissance reports, the vanguard of the Guangdong rebel Li Yangjing's troops has arrived at Pingshi, and the bulk of Xiang Hanping's forces are concentrated in Shaoguan, all transporting supplies northward. It is heard that Commander-in-Chief Jiang has always focused on peace and that the Hunan Army and other armies have strict defenses, so he is currently focused on suppressing the Red Army, striving to completely eliminate all the Red Bandits in the shortest possible time. He has temporarily decided not to transfer troops elsewhere. Currently, the bulk of Zhu, Mao, Peng, and Huang's forces are hoping to flee west across Jiangxi, intending to seize weapons in the border area of Hunan, Guangdong, and Jiangxi to reap the benefits. However, the left and right wings of the Suppression Army, in addition to pursuing the Red Bandits from Xingguo and Yudu, the Luo Lin and Gong Bingfan divisions are also deployed along the Gan River, such as Taihe and Wan'an, to block them. There are no other concerns. (August 5th)

External Report on Recent Diplomacy 50

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs yesterday (the 7th) dispatched Section Chief Bao Jing'an of the Intelligence Department to the Central Broadcasting Station to report on the recent diplomatic situation. His statement was as follows: (1) The Korean Anti-Chinese Incident: The most significant recent diplomatic event is the Korean Anti-Chinese incident. Due to the Japanese authorities' inadequate prevention beforehand and their failure to provide sufficient protection afterward, the lives and property of our country's overseas Chinese in Korea suffered extraordinarily significant losses. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has lodged a serious protest with the Japanese side. Ambassador Wang, stationed in Japan, who was ordered to go to Korea to investigate, has completed his inspection and is coming to Beijing to report everything. After receiving this report, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs should act in accordance with the Central Government's intentions and actively negotiate with Japan to achieve our desired goals. As for the Wanbaoshan incident, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is also consulting with the Jilin Provincial Government to carry out separate negotiations. (2) League of Nations Conference: The 12th regular session of the League of Nations will be held in Geneva next month. The National Government dispatched Shi Zhaoji, Minister to England, Jiang Zuobin, Minister to Germany, and Wang Jiazhen, Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, as representatives last month, with Minister Shi serving as the chief representative. Vice Minister Wang has already left Beijing for Harbin and will soon depart for Europe. Minister Jiang is expected to travel with Vice Minister Wang. As for the non-permanent council seat at this session, our country has high hopes, as we have been away from the League of Nations Administrative Council for three years. According to the election law passed in September 1926, we can be elected if we obtain more than half of the votes. Last year, our country requested re-election to the League of Nations, but according to the rules, it was necessary to obtain more than two-thirds of the votes to be elected. Therefore, our country received 27 votes last year, failing to be elected by a margin of five votes. If we can obtain the same number of votes at this session, which would be more than half, we should be able to be elected. However, our goal is to obtain a permanent council seat. (3) Recovery of the Mixed Court: The agreement on the establishment of a Chinese court in the French Concession of Shanghai was signed last week. The original text was published the day after the signing, and the French Concession's court was formally established on August 1st. The content of this agreement is largely the same as the Public Concession agreement established on February 17th of last year. However, there are one or two points that are even better. There are three Mixed Courts in China: the Shanghai Public Concession Court, the Shanghai French Concession Court, and the Gulangyu Court in Fujian. Now, the two Shanghai Courts have been recovered, leaving only the Gulangyu Court. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs is currently working on recovery measures. (4) Recovery of Concessions and Leased Territories: The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has been preparing for the recovery of concessions and leased territories for a long time. Regarding the recovery of the Guangzhouwan leased territory, we previously sent a note to the French side requesting them to send representatives to begin negotiations, but the French side has not yet made a definite response. As for the recovery of the Hankou Japanese Concession, we also previously sent a note to the Japanese government requesting them to send representatives to negotiate, but the Japanese side has not yet responded. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has recently sent another note to the Japanese side, requesting them to begin negotiations quickly. The other concessions that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is currently planning to recover include the public concessions of Wuhu and Gulangyu; the British concessions of Tianjin and Shamian; the French concessions of Tianjin, Shamian, Shanghai, and Hankou; the Italian concession of Tianjin; and the Japanese concessions in various locations. (5) Matters Concerning the Development of Overseas Chinese Affairs: It is the responsibility of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to protect overseas Chinese. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs' measures for protecting overseas Chinese are roughly divided into the following: (A) Negotiating with the governments of the host countries to remove obstacles to the conduct of overseas party affairs. (B) Negotiating the removal of various harsh regulations. (C) Coordinating the relief of unemployed Chinese laborers overseas. (D) Unifying the will of overseas Chinese to resolve the conflicts among Chinese societies in the Americas, in order to eliminate foreign anti-Chinese actions. (E) Rectifying overseas Chinese education. (F) Effectively promoting overseas Chinese registration to ensure thorough protection. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs is now actively pursuing these points separately. (6) Establishment of Consulates: In recent years, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has established many new consulates overseas, such as the Taipei Consulate General and the India Consulate General. Recently, a vice-consulate was established in Mazatlán, Mexico, and a consulate was established in Seattle, in the western United States. The Ministry is currently preparing to establish consulates in Saigon, Haiphong, Kuala Lumpur, Pontianak, Tahiti, and Timor. It also plans to establish consulates in Guatemala, Ecuador, Venezuela, Argentina, Colombia, Guyana, Haiti, Dominican Republic, Lourenço Marques in Portuguese East Africa, and Madagascar in French South Africa.

Japanese Consul Inspects the Situation of Overseas Chinese in Korea 51

The purpose is to investigate our oppression of Koreans

Since we have no oppressive acts, we might as well let them investigate

Jilin Correspondence: The Provincial Government previously received a telegram from Chief Zhou of the Changchun Municipal Office stating that an official from the Japanese Consulate in Changchun said that the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs planned to send Consul Yanai and Vice-Consul Wu of Liaoning to inspect Korean settlements in Changchun and other counties, hoping for protection. Considering that this is a tense time in the negotiations of the Wan-Korean and Korean-Chinese cases, it is worth noting what the purpose is for these consuls to suddenly come to our territory to freely investigate the situation of overseas Koreans. After requesting instructions from the Northeast Political Affairs Committee, we received a reply approving their visit, but they were not allowed to bring Japanese police officers. We would send police officers to accompany and monitor them, and the Commissioner of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Liaoning would forward the itinerary of the consuls to the government. On the 25th of last month, we telegraphed Chief Zhou to send personnel to accompany them and to inform the Public Security Bureau to send police to monitor them. At the same time, we sent copies of the telegram to the local officials of the places they would pass through and to the public security bureaus of the cities along the Binjiang River in the provincial capital, instructing them to immediately order the police to receive and protect them when the consuls arrived. We also ordered the police districts they would visit to earnestly protect them and to adopt a peaceful approach to the Korean incidents. The purpose of this trip by the consuls is probably to investigate the facts of Chinese oppression of Koreans, so that they can use it as a pretext for future negotiations with us. Therefore, we must pay close attention to what the consuls talk about with the Koreans after arriving in the villages and what attitude they take in their interactions. The counties concerned must send knowledgeable personnel to assist and secretly monitor them. If any Koreans hang or wave Japanese flags to welcome them, they should be strictly prohibited in advance. After the fact, the monitoring and all the interactions between the Japanese and Koreans should be reported in detail. It is reported that the consuls arrived in Changchun on July 25th and will continue to inspect various places. The inspection is expected to be completed in about a month, and they will depart from Jilin on August 28th on their way home. (August 2nd)

Recent Activities of Japanese Police in Wanbaoshan 52

Japanese Consul in Harbin Interferes with Public Opinion

Northeast Authorities Respond with Strong Words

Jilin Correspondence: The Provincial Authorities recently received a report from the Preparatory Office of the Changchun Municipal Government stating that several tents erected by Japanese police at Majiashao had been removed. The Japanese police officers had moved into nearby civilian homes, with only two or three tents remaining, all occupied by Koreans. On the surface, the situation seems to have eased somewhat, and our people have not taken any drastic actions. However, it is reported that the Japanese Consul General in Harbin recently sent a letter to our diplomatic officials, saying that our people's hearts are agitated and harming Sino-Japanese relations, which is quite alarming. The original letter roughly stated: "The Korean riots in various parts of Korea caused by the Wanbaoshan incident are regrettable to everyone. However, according to subsequent intelligence observations, all of Korea has returned to peace. The Governor-General of Korea is thoroughly investigating the rioters and providing relief to the victims. The overseas Chinese in various places have also gradually begun their businesses. However, the newspapers in your country have recently published exaggerated articles on this issue, dedicated to stirring up people's hearts, which is truly a regrettable phenomenon in Sino-Japanese relations. Moreover, it seems that the propaganda is being directed by the Japanese. It is also said that Koreans attacked the Chinese Consulate General in Gyeongseong, and Consul General Zhang took refuge in the Governor-General's residence, which can be said to be inhumane slander. Furthermore, this Consulate General has received telegrams from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Governor-General of Korea, which can further prove that the facts are unfounded and beyond doubt. However, according to reports in your country's newspapers, powerful public and private organizations in the area seem to believe in the above rumors and are issuing fiery telegrams or speeches, merely inciting the excitement of the masses. Among them, there are even those who advocate economic severance between China and Japan. If this is allowed to continue, I am convinced that there will be no good results in improving Sino-Japanese relations. In the future, please properly suppress such malicious propaganda and do not allow it to continue." Upon investigation, the occurrence of this Korean incident was due to the fabrication of rumors and the malicious propaganda of various provocations and incitements in the Japanese and Korean newspapers, which aroused the anger of the Koreans and led to such a major tragedy. However, the Japanese authorities have not been heard to have taken any action against their newspapers, but they regard our expressions of pent-up grievances and unfair opinions as malicious propaganda and suppress them. This is truly excessive intolerance. It is reported that our officials, after receiving this letter, have responded with strong words.

Statistics on Refugees Heading to Various Locations

The overseas Chinese who were accommodated have been completely assisted in leaving the country to seek a living in various places. According to the Magistrate of Andong County, if unemployed overseas Chinese from Korea continue to come to Andong, the Mao Hing Inn at Zhongfu Bridge will be designated as a place for overseas Chinese to stay, and they will be properly accommodated and assisted in leaving the country at any time to avoid displacement. The staff of the reception center handled the final closing matters on August 1st. The total number of people assisted is as follows: 75 people to Yantai, 33 to Dalian, 822 to Qingdao, 62 to Sinuiju, 22 to Weihai, 15 to Longkou, 66 to Shenyang, 5 to Tongyuanpu, 1 to Nanfen, 69 to Harbin, 11 to Changchun, 2 to Anda Station, 3 to Jilin, 3 to Liuzhan, 1 to Qianjinzai, 218 to Linjiang, 26 to Kuandian, 106 to Tonghua, 11 to Huanren, 12 to Antu, 95 to Changbai, 1 to Pyongyang, 1 to Qiaotou, 3 to Dingzhou, 13 to Dagushan, 116 staying in Andong, 2 to Sandaolangtou, 7 to Fushun, 220 to Tianjin, 4 to Longwangmiao. New Reforms of the South Manchuria Railway Company 54

All Power Concentrated in Shenyang

President Handles Diplomatic Affairs

Northeast Authorities Should Pay Close Attention

Andong Correspondence: Since Uchida and Eguchi succeeded as President and Vice-President of the South Manchuria Railway Company (SMR), the Japanese policy toward Manchuria and Mongolia has changed accordingly. It has been many days since Uchida and Eguchi took office. Their first step is to reform the SMR's organizational structure and personnel changes, which are described below:

Organizational Reform: The newly reformed SMR organizational structure has six departments - General Affairs, Management, Supervision, Railway, Local Affairs, and Commerce - and one Technical Bureau. The General Affairs Department directly manages five offices: the Tokyo Branch, the Fengtian Office, the Harbin Office, the Fushun Coal Mine, and the Anshan Iron Works. The Supervision Department has two sections: Investigation and Management. The Management Department has two sections: Budget and Accounting. The Railway Department has eight sections: General Affairs, Management, Operations, Joint Transportation, Rolling Stock, Engineering, Ports, and Electricity. The Local Affairs Department has seven sections: General Affairs, Local Affairs, Education, Commerce and Industry, Agriculture, Health, and Construction. The Fengtian Office under the General Affairs Department is particularly noteworthy. The Fengtian Office was originally the Fengtian Public Office. This time, it has been upgraded from the Fengtian Local Affairs Office to the Fengtian Office and is under the General Affairs Department. The General Affairs Department reports directly to the President. The SMR's negotiation affairs have been transferred to the management of the Fengtian Office, which means they will be handled directly by the SMR President. Therefore, all the power of the SMR will be concentrated in Shenyang. This is the most noteworthy aspect of this reform. Mr. Uchida is a well-known diplomat. From the beginning of his appointment, commentators said that he would demonstrate his diplomatic skills. This time, he resolutely placed the SMR's negotiation affairs under his iron fist. This is a new reform of the Japanese policy towards Manchuria and Mongolia in the past thirty years. The long-stagnant Northeast Railway negotiations, with the SMR's external power now shifted to Shenyang, may see a new situation develop as a result.

Personnel Changes: According to SMR tradition, whenever the President is replaced, all the staff are also changed. This time, with Uchida and Eguchi taking office, it is no different. The most important personnel changes this time include the replacement of the heads of the General Affairs, Management, and other departments with new personnel. The SMR's affiliated organizations, such as various schools, have also been changed. The new Director of the General Affairs Department is Mr. Yamauchi, the Director of the Management Department is Mr. Shuto, the Director of the Supervision Department is Mr. Takenaka, the Director of the Railway Department is Mr. Murakami, the Director of the Local Affairs Department is Mr. Omori, and the Director of the Commerce Department is Mr. Sogawa. The heads of local offices in various places have also been changed: Hiraoka Yasuo for Dashiqiao, Momma Kenichi for Yingkou, Kawasaki Inokichi for Anshan, Maeda Etsuo for Tieling, Ogawa Takuma for Kaiyuan, Mori Kageki for Gongzhuling, Yuoka Shigeru for Changchun, and Tada Akira for Andong. The staff of the Andong-Fengtian Railway have also been greatly changed, from stationmasters to drivers, all replaced with new personnel. The new stationmaster of Andong Station is Chiba Katsuo, and the former stationmaster, Orida Yushin, has been transferred to the Dalian Transportation Office. All the newly appointed personnel took office at the end of July and the beginning of this month. Therefore, recently, there have been many SMR personnel traveling back and forth on the South Manchuria and Andong-Fengtian Railways. (August 2nd)

Detailed Account of Wang Junjie's Murder of the Division Commander 55

Wang and those Involved in the Conspiracy Were All Captured

He Zhenfan Died Three Days After Being Shot

Hankou Correspondence: Wang Junjie, Brigade Commander of the 2nd Brigade of the 34th Division of the Army, plotted to seize military control of the division and assassinated He Zhenfan, the Acting Division Commander, on July 14th in the defense area of Xiantaozhen, as previously reported. He Chengjun, Director of the General Headquarters, believed that Wang's behavior was rebellious and that he should be dealt with according to the law to rectify military discipline. However, considering that Wang was leading troops in the defense area, and the division's mission area was distributed across more than 300 li of key areas in Xianmian, he was concerned that hasty action might have other impacts, so he temporarily tolerated him. After Wang killed He, he sent Yao Yingcheng, the division's adjutant, to Hankou to visit Director He, stating that He had died of illness and that Wang was maintaining the defense area, reluctantly complying with the request of all the division's officers to temporarily act as division commander and await further orders. Director He used the tactic of feigning leniency to entrap the enemy, speaking kindly to Yao and immediately appointing Wang Junjie as the Acting Division Commander of the 34th Division. He ordered Yao to personally bring the letter of appointment to the Xiantao defense area, instructing Yao to reassure Wang that he should secure the military, work hard to suppress the Communists, and that he would find special ways to provide whatever was needed. The General Headquarters' attitude towards Wang was seemingly extremely favorable. Yao deeply believed this and happily returned to Xiantao to report back, carrying Wang's appointment letter as Acting Division Commander of the 34th Division. Furthermore, Director He fully agreed to all the promotions recommended by Wang for battalion and brigade commanders, and decided to announce them according to procedure. Wang and his subordinates secretly congratulated each other and strongly urged Wang to come to Hankou to thank Director He. Soon after, Director He telegraphed Wang to come to Hankou for consultation. Wang was overwhelmed by this favor and, together with Yao Yingcheng, Wang's Chief of Staff Zhao Jizhi, the newly appointed Chief of Military Law Chen Boyan, and eleven followers, arrived in Hankou on August 3rd. On the morning of August 3rd, Wang, together with Yao Yingcheng, visited Director He at the General Headquarters. He was immediately arrested and handed over to the military law department. At the same time, personnel were dispatched to the World Hotel to arrest Zhao Jizhi, Chen Boyan, and the eleven followers, and they were detained in the military law department and the detective office. It is reported that the General Headquarters plans to organize a military tribunal to try this case. Director He has also telegraphed Commander-in-Chief Chiang regarding the details of handling this case, as Chiang is paying extraordinary attention to this case and has long instructed He to handle the case with full authority. As for the details of the case, it is said that Wang Junjie was indeed the mastermind behind He Zhenfan's murder. Those involved in the conspiracy included Wang's Chief of Staff Zhao Jizhi, the head of the pistol company Li Xiuzhi, and a person named Hu. The time of He Zhenfan's murder was 4:00 AM on July 14th. Wang initially ordered Zhao, Li, Hu, and others to lead their troops and surround He's residence before dawn. Then, they disarmed He's guards and imprisoned them. They dragged He out of bed and Wang, Zhao, Li, and others used their pistols to escort He to Wang's brigade headquarters. Along the way, they punched and kicked him, leaving him covered in bruises. At the time, He's only follower was a soldier named Liang Zixiu, who was unable to resist. Upon reaching the entrance of Wang's brigade headquarters, Wang first shot He in the lungs, with the bullet exiting his back. As He turned his head to speak, another bullet grazed his tongue and exited his left jaw. He cried out in pain, saying, "Please quickly aim at my head and give me a quick death." Another shot came, but it missed. At this time, Zhao and Li struggled to shoot soldier Liang, and a bullet entered his waist. Liang pretended to be dead. After everyone dispersed, he endured the pain and secretly fled to Hankou, where he secretly informed He Zhenfan's family and received treatment in the hospital. After Wang, Zhao, Li, and others shot and wounded He, seeing him lying on the ground bleeding profusely, they ignored him and sent their troops to guard the various organs of the division. At the same time, they detained Wang Wenshan, the division's chief of ordnance, Zhang Xianghe, the chief of military law, and Dong Fangting, the commander of the 2nd regiment, and Wang Jichang, the commander of the 6th regiment, who were summoned to Xiantao to attend the bandit suppression conference (the conference closed after three days). They fabricated telegrams to various places, falsely claiming in the name of all the officers that He Zhenfan had resigned due to illness and that the officers and soldiers had elected him as the acting division commander. They also guaranteed Hu as the commander of the 2nd regiment, Sun Yaowu as the commander of the 6th regiment, Li Xiuzhi, Xu, and others as battalion commanders, Chen Boyan as the chief of military law, and Dou as the chief of ordnance. They sealed off Xiantao, detained the post and telegraph, and cut off communication, so that the officers and soldiers of the division stationed in various places gradually learned the truth of the case after a long time. It is also reported that after He Zhenfan was shot and fell to the ground, he was still moaning in a pool of blood until 4:00 PM that day. After numerous officers and soldiers repeatedly requested it, Wang finally allowed him to be taken to the Xiantao Catholic Church, but he was still monitored and not allowed to eat or drink freely. He died at 7:00 PM on the 17th. However, on the 16th, He wrote two dying letters while lying in bed and secretly sent them to Hankou by a trusted aide, who presented them to two different offices. He did not pass away until the 17th. Upon investigation, Wang had previously murdered Liu Peng, the commander of the New 1st Division, in Yichang, and plotted to murder Li Yunlong, the commander of the New 3rd Division, in Dean. This time, killing He was the third time he had murdered a superior officer. Wang first betrayed Cao Wanshun, then betrayed Zhang Weixi, and betrayed Li Yunlong three times. This time, betraying He was the fourth time he had betrayed someone. He can truly be said to be rebellious by nature. (Night of August 5th)

The Anti-Shi Military is Preparing to Demobilize 56

Shi is Scattered Among the Disordered Troops and Military Operations will Conclude

Xuzhou Correspondence: According to the Security Department, the anti-Shi military operations are about to end. Since Shi's forces were surrounded and attacked by the Northeast Army and the Southern Route Group Army, there was no way out. After the Southern Route Army occupied Shijiazhuang and the Northeast Army occupied Dingzhou, Shi's forces scattered in the Cangshi Road area. The Pinghan Railway is now clear, and the Jinpu Railway has not yet been reached. The Wang Shuchang and Han Fuqu's troops blocked the west from Cangzhou and Dezhou, and the forward units of Shang Zhen's Jin Army will exit Niangziguan and head east. Shi is in a critical and isolated encirclement. Therefore, after the battle of Shijiazhuang, Shi fled with the disorderly troops. His whereabouts are currently unknown. The remainder of his forces, in addition to those who were disarmed and captured, may be reorganized by Han Fuqu. The Commander-in-Chief of the Southern Route Army, Liu Zhi, has arrived in Shunde, and Gu Zhutong is accompanying the army to the front. Wang Jun inspected the Daoqing Line, and the troops are advancing. However, since the military operations have been concluded, the main forces will soon demobilize. The various units of the 3rd Army Corps may soon return south. Qian Zongze, the transportation commander of the Jinlong and Pingdao Four Routes, telegraphed Yin Dihuang, the director of the Pukou Office, on the 5th, stating that the rebel Shi had been fundamentally resolved, the military operations had been concluded, and the main forces were urgently awaiting demobilization. All military supplies in the rear should cease to be transported forward to avoid wasted effort. Empty trains should be prepared and concentrated between Xuzhou and Guide to prepare for military transport. In particular, the Guard Army should be limited to concentrating in Pukou before steam. On the same day (the 5th), the 3rd Independent Artillery Regiment, which was heading north from Pukou, was ordered to turn back. The forward units are also being mobilized for demobilization. (August 6th)

Page 10

The Wei Lihuang Division Enters Fujian from Jiangxi to Suppress Bandits 57

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Fujian Red Bandits, led by Luo Zhu and others, have repeatedly requested the Central Government to send more troops to Fujian for a joint suppression. It is reported that the Central Government has dispatched the Wei Lihuang Division to enter Fujian from Jiangxi. They will first meet with Zhang Zhen's division in western Fujian to eliminate the remaining Reds in Tinglong and other places. Then, they will meet with the Provincial Government and the various armies to reorganize military and political affairs. The expenses for bandit suppression will be provided by the Central Government. The Provincial Government has telegraphed its welcome and urged them to come as soon as possible. The Provincial Government has also ordered the Lu Division to go to Liancheng and Changting to fill the defenses. Commander-in-Chief Chiang has also ordered the Lu Division to arrive before the 5th of this month. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, the refugees from Changting petitioned the Provincial Government for three things: (1) to quickly find ways to accommodate the refugees from Tingzhou scattered in various places; (2) to quickly send a large army to recover the counties of Changting; and (3) to quickly allocate funds to relieve the refugees in Tingzhou who have suffered from the disaster. (August 4th)

The Hunan Provincial Government Newly Formulates a Prohibition Plan 58

Current Tobacco Tax is Approaching One Million

Changsha Correspondence: A large amount of tobacco soil is transported to Hunan from Guizhou every year for sale. Therefore, the government has specially established a special tax clearing office to collect special taxes. A special tax of 400 yuan is levied on each dan of tobacco soil, excluding the protection fee. The total monthly revenue is about 600,000 to 700,000 yuan, and can reach more than 1 million yuan in peak months. Originally, half was handed over to the Ministry of Finance and half was retained by Hunan as military expenses. Later, due to the difficulty of military expenses in Hunan, He Jian requested and was approved by the Central Government that all of this special tax, starting from July, would be retained in Hunan for military expenses and no longer handed over to Beijing. Tobacco soil that has been affixed with flowers and paid taxes can be openly sold, which greatly hinders the prospects of tobacco prohibition. Recently, the Hunan Provincial Party Affairs Guidance Committee telegraphed the Central Government, requesting it to resolutely abolish the Hunan special tax in order to eliminate the poison. Whether this will be approved has not yet been received. However, the Hunan Provincial Government has formulated an administrative outline for the 20th year, which was passed at the provincial affairs meeting the other day. For the tobacco prohibition measures for the 20th year, eight items are stipulated, which will be reported to the Central Government and promulgated for implementation. According to the various items stipulated in the measures, such as prohibiting planting, transporting, selling, and smoking, Guizhou tobacco soil can no longer be transported to Hunan in the future, and the so-called special tax has been fundamentally abolished. However, the military expenses of the 4th Army Corps rely entirely on special taxes for funding. Although the tobacco prohibition measures have been passed by the provincial government, whether they can be implemented depends entirely on whether the military agrees. The measures are recorded as follows: (1) Supervise and order the entire province to strictly prohibit opium. (2) Select personnel to inspect tobacco prohibition in various cities and counties. (3) Strictly examine the achievements of tobacco prohibition personnel and reward or punish them accordingly. (4) Plan to establish a provincial tobacco prohibition committee. (5) Prohibition of planting: 1. Strictly prohibit the planting of poppies. 2. Order areas planting tobacco to implement the replacement of various agricultural crops. 3. Strictly order the county magistrates to conduct on-site inspections of tobacco seedlings. 4. Select personnel to review tobacco seedlings. (6) Prohibition of transportation: 1. Strictly prohibit the import of tobacco soil. 2. Inspect boats and vehicles for privately transported opium. 3. Strictly order public security agencies to identify merchants transporting tobacco soil and order them to issue a written pledge never to transport tobacco soil. (7) Prohibition of sales: 1. Strictly prohibit the manufacture and sale of tobacco soil and smoking paraphernalia, and seal off their business premises. 2. Search for hidden tobacco soil, residual膏, and smoking paraphernalia, confiscate and destroy them. (8) Prohibition of smoking: 1. Strictly prohibit the opening of brothels for people to smoke opium. 2. Those who are caught smoking opium will be ordered to quit smoking within a limited time. 3. Supervise and urge various cities and counties to establish addiction treatment centers and addiction treatment clinics, and encourage individuals or groups to establish addiction treatment clinics. 4. Crack down on addiction treatment drugs. 5. Review the use of the 20% of addiction treatment funds spent by various cities and counties. 6. Implement drug testing for civil servants. 7. Plan to establish a civil servant drug testing center. 8. Strictly order the waterway and land public security agencies to investigate tobacco offenders. (August 1st)

Qingdao

Repercussions of the Bureau of Standards, Metrology and Inspection's Excessive and Harsh Inspections 59

Qingdao Chamber of Commerce and Various Trade Associations

Request the Control Yuan to Dispatch Personnel for Thorough Investigation and Strict Punishment

Qingdao Correspondence: The Qingdao Bureau of Standards, Metrology and Inspection has previously implemented improper inspection procedures, causing dissatisfaction among merchants, leading to repeated strikes and business closures. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce and various trade associations, due to Bureau Chief Mou Junde's disregard for public opinion, excessive and harsh inspections, have seen their industries decline daily, which is contrary to the original intention of the state in establishing the bureau. Therefore, they decided in a meeting yesterday to jointly send a telegram to the Control Yuan to file a complaint, requesting the dispatch of personnel to thoroughly investigate the bureau's accounts and severely punish them to maintain commerce. The original text of the telegram is recorded below: To President of the Nanjing Control Yuan: The Qingdao Bureau of Standards, Metrology and Inspection's excessive and harsh inspections are harming merchants and the people. We earnestly request the dispatch of personnel for thorough investigation to ensure its reputation matches its reality and to alleviate the distress of Jiangsu merchants. Upon investigation, the establishment of the Bureau of Standards, Metrology and Inspection was originally intended to improve products and increase credibility. The inspection fees charged should only be sufficient to cover inspection expenses and should not be comparable to a national tax collection agency. Taking from merchants and using for merchants is clearly stated in official documents and known throughout the country. However, Bureau Chief Mou Junde and others are greedy and exacting, imposing harsh levies. At the beginning of operations, they still knew to adhere to some boundaries, but in recent years, they have intensified and acted recklessly, using the name of inspection to secretly pursue private collection of fees. For example, crude oil is charged nine cents per dan, soybean oil nine cents per dan, peanut kernels five cents per dan, peanuts three cents per dan, cotton six cents per dan, peanut cake one cent per dan, pork one yuan and six jiao per dan, egg products three cents per dan, fresh eggs two cents per thousand, live cattle five jiao per head, raw cowhide five jiao and five fen per dan, frozen cowhide five jiao per dan, beef tallow two jiao per dan, and wool nine jiao per dan. Based on the quantity of the above items transported and sold to various places by the Jiaohai Customs in the 19th year, the inspection fees collected should amount to more than 300,000 yuan. As for silkworm cocoons, tobacco leaves, soybeans, and coarse grains, none are spared. Furthermore, the bureau often uses inspection as a pretext to extract samples of goods in large quantities, causing losses to merchants and people who dare not complain. They must not only pay various huge amounts of money but also suffer various harsh and cumbersome disturbances. Even the pork needed for daily use by the people of this city is subject to inspection fees, but in reality, no inspection is ever carried out; only personnel are sent to collect fees without issuing formal receipts, which is even more shocking. It is estimated that the annual amount of illegally collected fees is no less than 400,000 yuan. Under the name of an inspection agency, they are actually acting as a collection agency, which has repeatedly aroused strikes and business closures by members of various trade associations, with significant direct and indirect consequences. Their appeals have been ignored. Guangzhou, Shanghai, Hankou, Tianjin, and other places have all established bureaus, but there have been no reports of such harsh treatment. Without even the need for promotion, Qingdao's commerce has already been almost completely destroyed by Mou Junde and others' deceptive tactics and cruel flames of greed. In a state of urgency and desperation, we jointly send this telegram to earnestly request your esteemed Yuan to promptly dispatch personnel to thoroughly investigate the bureau's accounts and severely punish them to rectify official conduct and maintain commerce. We are filled with anticipation and await your orders. Qingdao Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Native Products Merchants Association, Pork Trade Association, Egg Trade Association, Cigarette Trade Association, Cotton Yarn Trade Association, Chinese and Foreign Cotton Cloth Trade Association, Money Trade Association, Restaurant Trade Association, Shipping Trade Association, Transportation Trade Association, General Merchandise Merchants Association, Silk and Satin Cloth Merchants Association, Straw Hat Weaving Trade Association, Inn Trade Association, Yellow Wine Trade Association, Banking Trade Association, Liquor Trade Association, Automobile Trade Association, Coal Trade Association, etc., respectfully kowtow. (August 1st)

Wuhu Express News 60

Dangtu County, which is connected to Wuhu, has 900,000 mu of fertile land. The largest, Daguan Embankment, occupies 480,000 mu. Since the major flood, the villagers of the entire embankment have exerted their utmost efforts to prevent breaches and have preserved it until now. Unexpectedly, the embankment, which had been submerged for a long time, suddenly collapsed the night before last. Although the villagers tried to save it by beating gongs, it was impossible to recover. The breach caused a disaster, flooding more than 600,000 mu of land in the surrounding embankments, resulting in huge losses.

The flood in Anhui Province is unprecedented in decades. Southern Anhui is the primary rice-producing region in the country, and the losses are even greater. In addition to the Wuhu Flood Relief Association, people from various counties residing in Wuhu initiated the establishment of the Wuhu, Xuancheng, Nanling, and Fanchang Four-County Relief Association yesterday to cooperate fully. The founding meeting was held at the county government, and Zhai Zhancheng, Yu Bohua, and ten others were elected as committee members to raise donations from inside and outside the province and organize work relief.

Due to the severe flooding in Wuhu, the fields and crops have been almost completely submerged, and there is no source for land tax or educational surcharges. The county's education system is facing bankruptcy. The Education Bureau and the Education Promotion Association have held meetings for days and resolved to levy entertainment taxes and streetlight pole surcharges, and also plan to close down elementary schools in various rural areas, as the embanked fields have become a waterland and the farmers cannot settle down and even if they did, it would be futile.

Since raising dozens of yuan in relief funds, the Wuhu Flood Relief Association has been hiring boats to distribute money, rice, and bread to provide temporary relief. To devise a fundamental solution, it has divided into groups to investigate the number of disaster victims and the flooding of embanked fields. Zhao, the head of the Public Security Bureau, and others took a boat to various villages yesterday to investigate. In addition, the association has nominated committee member He Wuzi to go to Shanghai today to request urgent relief from Xu Shiying, chairman of the Central Relief Committee.

Defense in Wuhu has been tightened in recent days. The police authorities specially sent people to announce to residents last night that firecrackers are prohibited from 6:00 PM to 6:00 AM, because pirates have been rampant across the river for days, and the sound of gunfire continues throughout the night, causing unease. Robbery cases have sprung up in the four townships like bees. The Shiwei Town Public Security mistakenly killed five thieves yesterday. The county government has arrested even more people in recent days. Xie Caixing and Yang Jiahe were executed last night. The 271st Brigade Headquarters dispatched troops across the river last night to patrol. (June 6th)

Wuxi 63

Attention to Southern Opera: Since the spring of this year, the film industry has been flourishing in Wuxi's entertainment venues, followed by Southern Opera. There are more than a dozen places inside and outside the city, most of which are temporary reed sheds built on open ground, using obscene lyrics and seductive melodies to attract ordinary men and women, laborers, and young people. The Wuxi Municipal Management Committee has repeatedly received letters from the Provincial Education Institute requesting a ban. Yesterday, it specifically sent a letter to the County Construction Bureau and the County Public Security Bureau, requesting that these reed sheds where many people gather be strictly banned, as such poor entertainment can hinder public morals. If such a situation occurs, it is hoped that the Public Security Bureau will immediately ban it, revoke the licenses at any time, and order the industry to cease operations to maintain public morals and serve as a warning.

Strict Prohibition of Raising Rice Prices: County Magistrate Chen has repeatedly received reports from Qian Zhongliang, the district head of the first district, stating that the county has suffered a major flood, and the low-lying fields have been completely submerged, but rice merchants are raising rice prices, increasing by more than one yuan per dan. Some are hoarding and speculating, affecting society and causing unrest, requesting a strict ban on exporting rice and ordering rice merchants not to raise prices or hoard, but to sell at fair prices to benefit the common people. Yesterday, a proclamation was specially issued, and personnel were dispatched daily to investigate and report on the grain market situation and rice reserves for regulation.

Yixing Zhangzhu Town Murder and Kidnapping Case: According to news from the transportation sector yesterday, Lu Chunda, a villager in Zhangzhu Bashan Village, Yixing, was over sixty years old. His family had considerable land. He had two sons. At about 6:00 AM the day before yesterday, Chunda planned to go to the nearby mountains to cut bamboo to sell at the market. Unexpectedly, on the way, he encountered seven bandits, each holding long guns, box cannons, and other weapons, ordering him to stop and not to move. Chunda, seeing the situation, shouted for help, angering the bandits, who pulled out a box cannon, and with a bang, a bullet hit his temple, and he fell to the ground and died. The bandits then fled towards Shi'ao Lake and Gongling. Afterwards, passersby glimpsed Lu Chunda being killed by bandits and immediately reported to his family, who in turn reported to the Zhangzhu Chamber of Commerce and various village self-defense corps, who immediately dispatched members armed with guns to pursue, but the bandits had already fled far away. Furthermore, Chen Xida and Chen Songda, residents of Shengzhuang Village, about fifteen or sixteen li from Zhangzhu Town, were kidnapped by a large gang of bandits on the 15th of last month and imprisoned in the bandit's den. The Chen family was extremely anxious. Recently, the bandits sent a letter stating that Chen Xida's ransom was 7,000 yuan and Chen Songda's ransom was 3,000 yuan, and they demanded quick payment. After receiving the letter, the Chen family, being impoverished, could not raise the money and ignored it. It is heard that after kidnapping the two hostages, the bandits found that the Chen family was indeed poor, so Chen Songda alone was safely released from the bandit's den.

Capture of Taixing Bandit Leader in Changzhou: The Taixing County Police Team learned that the county's bandit leader had fled to Changzhou under the alias Zhou Bing, residing at the Zhonghua Hotel at the entrance of Hualong Lane. On the 6th, they dispatched Special Agent Xu Rongting to lead a team to Changzhou to arrest him. County Magistrate Zhang also sent a detective team to assist. They immediately rushed to surround and arrest him, and indeed captured him in the opera house. He was taken to the detective team and is scheduled to be taken back to Taixing for interrogation on the 8th.

Murder Case in Lotus Village in the Northern Suburbs: Pan Chanda, 53 years old, of Lotus Village outside the North Gate of Wuyi, suffered from mental illness. The night before last, his younger brother, Anjin, tied his hands with rope and chained him to the well railing in the yard with an iron chain. At this time, Chanda was still stubborn, so Anjin pressed a waterwheel awning on his body. The next day, when they checked, Chanda had already died. The incident was learned by the police nearby, who dispatched police on the 6th to arrest Anjin for transfer to the interrogation office.

Zhenjiang 65

Water Level in the Canal Drops Slightly After Opening the Dams: Since the Xinche and Liangba dams were opened, the water level in the canal has dropped slightly. On the 5th, Mao, the director of the Water Conservancy Bureau, and the resident engineering committee members of the provincial government reported to the province from Gaoyou that the Nanguan Dam was impacted by wind and waves and was overflowing, which was no different from opening it, and requested it be put on record. In the afternoon, the water receded by three fen, with a water level of one zhang, nine chi, and seven fen. It was also reported that two of the four dams under the Gaoyou moat were leaking and were being urgently protected. The Jiangsu Provincial Water Conservancy Bureau received telegrams from Gaoyou yesterday and today, requesting 10,000 hemp bags, which have been loaded in batches and sent to Gaoyou for use under escort. The dikes are currently being protected day and night by Water Conservancy Bureau personnel supervising local officials and civilians, as well as the Yunhe defense army and police, to prevent collapse. However, the original long-distance telephone along the Yunhe is too far away, and the transmission of information is not timely enough. The Construction Department has telegraphed the Ministry of Communications' Directorate General of Telecommunications to request the addition of ten telephones at important locations along the Yunhe to facilitate defense.

Provincial Security Office Pays Attention to Banditry in Jiangbei: The Provincial Security Office, concerned about frequent bandit disturbances along the coast of Jiangbei, in addition to designating the reorganized Shen Fengshan's maritime guerrilla force to patrol the sea area in the Yancheng and Funing areas, ordered the counties of Tongzhou and Taizhou to quickly organize a water patrol team and reorganize the original fishing groups in each field. As for coastal transportation, the existing Fan Dike will be used to expand and build a highway. Once approved by the provincial government and the pacification commissioner, the road will be built by soldiers and workers. The office recently received a telegram from the Funing government stating that banditry in the county is rampant and the people are suffering, requesting the swift dispatch of capable troops to suppress them. Yesterday, it specifically consulted with Commander Liang of the 25th Route Army to dispatch troops nearby to suppress them severely.

Second Appraisal of Yi Wang's Lawsuit: Merchant Yi Ruichang, previously suffering from a joint disease, sought treatment at the Provincial Hospital. Because the bone was broken and he could not move, he filed a lawsuit against Wang Yuanchen, the director of the hospital, for negligence of duty leading to disability at the local court. After the Hongren Hospital appraisal proved the surgery was a mistake, Wang stated that he was not present at the time of the appraisal and could not be relied upon, requesting a new appraisal. The court hired Zhang Xiong from the Suzhou Bu Xiong Hospital to Zhenjiang to perform a second appraisal using the Hongren Aix's mirror yesterday. Both the plaintiff and the defendant were summoned. Once Dr. Zhang's report is received by the court, a public debate will be held.

In addition to reporting the case to the province for approval yesterday, it also issued an order to the various public security bureaus, requiring them to deliver at least five opium addicts to the institute for forced detoxification within two weeks.

It has been a long time and has not been settled. The Finance Department has repeatedly ordered him to pay. The Finance Department believes that this salary withdrawal was not reported at the time and was not included in the handover records. It has been more than two years before verification was requested. After the Finance Department ordered the county to investigate, Yan, the former county magistrate, replied according to Xu Qingbiao's letter that the previous withdrawals were 6,900 yuan from the miscellaneous tax office's deposits that had not been turned over to the treasury, 7,400 yuan from local funds, and 6,700 yuan borrowed and advanced, totaling 21,000 yuan, and reported to the Finance Department for verification. Now, former County Magistrate Xu has again submitted a detailed list of the military salary loans for verification. The Finance Department, to determine whether the amounts are consistent, ordered the county Finance Bureau yesterday to investigate in detail, and ordered former County Magistrate Xu to rush to Jiaxing for a joint settlement and report, so that they can verify.

Nearly a Riot in the Disaster Area in the Western Countryside: The villages of Zixia, Taoyuan, and Shahe in the southern countryside of Xiaoshan were flooded by continuous heavy rains and flash floods last month, resulting in the drowning of rice seedlings. Educational News

Important News 74

Overview of Secondary Education in Guangdong Province 75

Statistics on Secondary Schools and Students in the Province

In recent years, secondary education in Guangdong Province has seen considerable expansion, especially in the number of secondary schools. However, there has been no accurate statistical data on the gradual increase in secondary schools across the province. Recently, the Department of Education began conducting surveys. The following is a summary of the findings, providing a glimpse into the state of secondary education in Guangdong Province in the coming year: "Provincial" (1) Guangzhou Provincial First Middle School: 408 male students across all grades, 109 graduates; (2) Guangzhou Provincial Second Middle School: 465 male students in grades 1, 2, 3, and 6, 169 graduates; (3) Huiyang County Provincial Third Middle School: 279 male students in grades 1, 2, and 3, 422 graduates; (4) Chao'an County Provincial Fourth Middle School: 279 male students and 36 female students in grades 1, 2, 3, 4, and 5, 57 male graduates and 9 female graduates; (5) Meixian County Provincial Fifth Middle School: 1,392 male students and 58 female students across all grades, 180 male graduates; (6) Nanxiong County Provincial Sixth Middle School: 85 male students in grades 1 and 2, 23 male graduates; (7) Gaoyao County Provincial Seventh Middle School: 117 male students in grades 1, 2, and 3, 36 male graduates; (8) Luoding County Provincial Eighth Middle School: 888 male students and 12 female students in grades 1, 2, and 3, 45 male graduates and 4 female graduates; (9) Maoming County Provincial Ninth Middle School: 264 male students and 5 female students in grades 1, 2, and 3, 51 male graduates and 1 female graduate; (10) Haikang County Provincial Tenth Middle School: 115 male students in grades 1, 2, and 3, 317 graduates; (11) Hepu County Provincial Eleventh School: 405 male students and 38 female students in grades 1, 2, 3, 4, and 5, 90 male graduates and 5 female graduates; (12) Qin County Provincial Twelfth Middle School: 101 male students and 10 female students in grades 1, 2, and 3, 27 male graduates and 1 female graduate; (13) Qiongdong County Provincial Thirteenth Middle School: 265 male students and 2 female students in grades 1, 2, and 3, 98 male graduates and 1 female graduate; (14) Guangzhou Provincial First Girls' Middle School: 291 students in grades 1, 2, 3, and 4. The total for all provincial middle schools is 4,363 male students, 432 female students, 1,623 male graduates, and 21 female graduates. Educational Institutions Should Monthly

Compile Three Copies of Monthly Payment Budget 78

The Ministry of Education, in accordance with a letter from the Ministry of Finance, requires all schools and educational institutions to compile three copies of their monthly payment budget and submit them to the Ministry. A special notice is issued to all directly affiliated schools and educational institutions. The case is based on a letter from the Ministry of Finance stating, "Article 2 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Auditing Law stipulates that all government agencies should, before the 15th of each month, prepare a budget for payments for the following month, based on the scope of the budget, and submit it to the Ministry of Finance for review before forwarding it to the Auditing Yuan for record-keeping." Now that the 20th year has already begun, all temporary relief measures for when the budget has not been established have been approved by the National Government's Order No. 338. A copy of the relief measures is enclosed for your Ministry's review and to be forwarded to all affiliated schools and institutions to compile three copies of their monthly payment budget in accordance with the above-mentioned measures and the regulations of the detailed rules, and submit them to the Ministry for review and forwarding. This is hereby approved." After reviewing the above-mentioned temporary relief measures, they were already circulated for compliance under this Ministry's Order No. 1211 on July 17. Now that the above has been approved, it is hereby ordered to comply. This order.

Ministry of Education Seeks University Arithmetic Lecture Notes 80

For the Purpose of Compiling and Translating Mathematical Terminology

The Ministry of Education is seeking lecture notes from universities for the purpose of compiling and translating mathematical terminology. A special notice is being sent to all national universities, and educational departments and bureaus in all provinces and cities are being instructed to forward this request to all private universities to collect arithmetic lecture notes. The original order states, "Due to the Ministry's Terminology Translation Committee compiling and translating mathematical terminology, there is an urgent need for reference to the lecture notes used by various universities in this field. The following categories should be listed separately: (1) Chinese arithmetic lecture notes used in pre-courses; (2) Chinese arithmetic lecture notes used in public elective courses for non-science undergraduates, as well as Chinese arithmetic lecture notes for remedial courses; (3) Chinese arithmetic lecture notes for university science and engineering courses below integral calculus. Please submit one copy of each of the above to the Ministry as required. This order."

Local News 81

Labor University Strives to Revitalize 82

Implement Part-Work, Part-Study

Realize the Spirit of Labor

Since the students of the National Labor University underwent re-registration and strict review, the internal administration has also been greatly revitalized. Starting from the autumn semester, the university will vigorously implement the principle of part-work, part-study to realize the spirit of labor. President Wang Jingqi has invited the heads of the Industrial Society, Agricultural College, and Factory, Tang Ying, Zhang Yuanruo, Han Yanmen, factory director Li Yingbiao, and farm director Ma Shouzhen to hold repeated meetings. It has been decided that in addition to internship work, students must do sixteen hours of production work per week. A work committee will be established to specifically guide, plan, and evaluate work. The president will serve as the chairman of the committee. At the end of each semester, each student must obtain a work certificate from the work committee before participating in the semester and graduation examinations. Those with poor work performance will not be allowed to participate. During work hours, instructors and students must wear blue work uniforms. The types of work are divided into approximately five categories: 1. Industrial Affairs Group: manufacturing, civil engineering, etc.; 2. Agricultural Affairs Group: farm production and promotion, etc.; 3. Public Affairs Group: water, electricity, school firefighting, etc.; 4. Education Group: translation, editing, printing, etc.; 5. Investigation Group: social statistics, etc. Each group will have a director concurrently serving as a committee member. A school affairs meeting will also be held soon to decide on all major policies for the start of the academic year, so that the school can keep up with the times.

Principal Li Bojun Transferred to Changhe and An 84

The Educational Society reports that Principal Li Bojun of Shanghai Municipal Yangzheng School has served as principal for three years, achieving remarkable results. Just as he was planning to continue making progress and working hard for the school, he received an order from the bureau to transfer to Changhe and An. Principal Li, due to years of accumulated hard work and poor health, repeatedly requested to resign, but his request was denied. All teachers, staff, students, alumni, and initiators of the school unanimously petitioned the Education Bureau to approve his exemption from the transfer. The Education Bureau, prioritizing education in the concession, did not approve the request. It is now reported that Principal Li will be heading to take up his new post within days. Thousands of students and their families have been going to the school to bid him farewell in recent days. Qian Xuanqing, the original principal of Changhe and An, will be transferred to Yangzheng at the same time.
