World Female Track and Field Star

Reason for Kinue Hitomi's Death 99

Dramatic Speech Leads to Serious Illness... Not Death Due to Exercise 100

(Osaka Dispatch) Japan's world-renowned track and field star, Miss Kinue Hitomi, unfortunately passed away due to a sudden onset of pneumonia at 0:25 PM on the 2nd of this month, as previously reported in this newspaper. Her death was largely suspected to be due to overexertion, causing concern for female athletes in general. However, the lady's death was definitely caused by the strenuous speeches she delivered across Japan after returning from the Third World Women's Games in Czechoslovakia last year. Due to lack of rest, her lungs were damaged, and she subsequently contracted pleurisy. Her condition gradually worsened, and she was admitted to Osaka Medical University Hospital for treatment in April of this year. She showed slight improvement by the end of May, but her body continued to weaken. Despite proper care, the disease had penetrated deep into her bones. Suddenly, on the afternoon of January 1st, a critical change occurred, and her life was in danger. Doctors administered dozens of cardiac stimulants, which prolonged her life until the following day. At the moment of her death, she still showed her indomitable spirit, writing a final note, saying, "Victory and defeat are things of the past; a chest ailment has taken my life." Her remains were cremated at the Osaka Abe Crematorium on the afternoon of the 3rd. The lady was born on January 1, 1907, originally from Fukuhama Village, Mitake County, Okayama Prefecture, as the second daughter of Mr. Inosaku Hitomi. She graduated from Okayama Prefectural Girls' High School in 1924. In 1925, she entered Nikaido Gymnastics and Women's School but did not graduate. Later, she served as a gymnastics teacher at Kyoto Girls' High School. In April 1926, she entered Japan Women's College of Physical Education, but withdrew the following year to become a correspondent for the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun. In August, she participated in the Second World Women's Games in Sweden, winning first place in the individual overall score and breaking four world records, thus making her name known worldwide. After returning to her country, she became an employee of the Mainichi Shimbun. In 1928, she attended the Ninth World Games, and last year, she also attended the Third World Women's Games in Czechoslovakia, winning every time. She held one-third of the world records, and almost all of the Japanese records were kept by her.

Page 11

Free Talk

World Snippets 101

— Seake

Color and Aroma Therapy

The medical field in Europe always has new inventions for treating diseases every year. Recently, a medical scientist invented a new method of treating mental illness by using colors and aromas, supplemented with medication. It is said to be very effective.

Eat as Much as You Want

Several restaurants in New York, for company dinners, never allowed extra dishes beyond what was listed on the menu. Recently, to attract customers, they changed the method. If there is something delicious in a company meal, customers can ask the restaurant to add more of it and eat as much as they want without extra charge. Since the implementation of this method, the business has flourished, but only 5% of customers have asked for a second serving. So there is not much loss.

Mechanical Artificial Respiration

People who drown or suffer from carbon monoxide poisoning often experience suffocation. It is necessary to quickly use artificial respiration to save them. In the past, there was no machinery for artificial respiration. Now, Britain has a machine that allows the patient to lie in a tight, airtight tank with only their head exposed. Air enters and exits within a specified short period, gradually restoring their breathing.

In Memory of My Late Friend, Ye Ziping Zhong 102

— Hu Pengfei

Sima Xiangru said, "A thousand gold sons do not sit under a dangerous eave." It is because their lives are precious, and they dare not lightly tread into danger or face unexpected events. How could my friend Ye Ziping Zhong, a scion of a noble family, forget this warning and playfully indulge in Fucha's water games, only to follow Qu Yuan's long journey, leaving eternal regret? Ziping Zhong's given name was Dan, and he was from Zhouzhuang near Suzhou. He was the second son of Mr. Ye Chucang, the chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government. At the age of seventeen, he studied at Shanghai Nanyang Middle School for many years. He was kind and approachable, not tainted by current habits. He was always diligent in his studies and devoted himself to school affairs selflessly. Therefore, he was highly respected by his classmates. He served as chairman of the class meeting and minister of the Department of Moral Education. His achievements were remarkable. Ye Zi always bravely stepped forward in matters relating to the class, never retreating slightly. He was fond of learning and thinking deeply about his studies, always ranking at the top of his class. Last winter's exam, because his physics score was slightly inferior, he worked harder this spring and finally ranked at the top. Not only were his classmates delighted, but his teachers also praised him. After class, he studied various ideologies and theories. Whenever he gained insight, he would write articles of thousands of words, neglecting sleep and food. He especially loved poetry. His works were often seen on the school's bulletin board. A few days ago, he sent me four seven-character quatrains, written after reading the novel "A Laughing Story." He was sincere and devoted to friendship. He was modest in his discussions of art and learning. He had the demeanor of a son of Shangqiu. Now, he has suddenly drowned while swimming. How can I not be saddened by this bad news? Ye Zi was not good at swimming. The first time he swam was this summer, on the Sunday before the big exam, when he practiced with his classmates at the Hongkou swimming pool. Unexpectedly, after returning to the town, he went into the water in the canal. He did not think of the words of Zichan, "Water is weak, and playing with it leads to death," and thus never recovered. Feng Yi raged and destroyed my good friend. Oh, destiny! Looking back to last winter, I traveled to Jingkou with my two younger brothers, Wu Zizhaozong and Yifei. After arriving in the town, we visited Ye Zi. We received a warm welcome and enjoyed the scenic spots of Jinshan, Jiaoshan, and Beigushan together. Although the north wind was fierce and the snow had just stopped, Ye Zi guided us warmly without any difficulty. We traveled for two days without separating. If I come again in the future, the scenery will be the same, but the man and his music will be gone. How can I not be heartbroken? I remember when we parted during the summer vacation, Ye Zi still asked about the date of my revisit to Jingkou. I told him that I would definitely go to the town during this holiday for a ten-day visit. How could I know that the words were still in my ears, but Poseidon took my old friend away? The past is like yesterday. I am heartbroken. Therefore, I wrote two odes to remember my old friend to express my pain. "Grief overflows. The friendship in the study window is deep, but the fate is shallow. Yangguan's song has just been sung, but sorrow is already foretold. How can I not be confused upon hearing the rumors? From now on, who will accompany me by the lamp and the cockcrow? Remembering our time together, my heart is broken. The waves cannot wash away my sorrow. Heaven's questions are unanswered. The setting sun turns to the west." "Playing in the clear waves, he followed Qu Yuan to the Miluo River. Zhong Qi is gone, and there are few who understand my music. The sound of the guqin is desolate. The two points of Jinshan and Jiaoshan are still the same. How can I bear to mention them again? I hear the tide rushing through the fog. I mourn my lost companions. I look at the Jingjiang River as far as the eye can see. Where can I call back his soul?" (Que Chou)

The Road is Like a Tiger's Mouth 103

— Zhenghong

The origin of the name "road" is difficult to trace. In terms of its meaning, a road is actually a path for horses to travel on. But those who rub shoulders and come and go busily, are they people or horses? Considering the name, one can't help but smile wryly. In the past, the Zhou road was as smooth as a whetstone and as straight as an arrow. Today's road is as smooth and straight as the Zhou road. But it is not called a "main road" but a "horse road." Even scholars and officials are accustomed to calling it that and do not notice it. This is also strange. Some say that a road is named so because the road is flat and wide enough to accommodate the galloping of angry horses. The meaning of the name "road" lies in this.

During my leisure time, I often stroll on the road. I often see the road authorities prominently displaying alarming slogans: "The road is like a tiger's mouth. Pedestrians must not walk on it." I think to myself, since it is called a "road," it is appropriate that people should not walk on it. But why is it compared to a tiger's mouth? I am confused. In the past, people used to walk instead of riding in carriages. The roads they walked on were not as flat and wide as today's roads. But today, people live in an age of material civilization, yet they cannot walk on the flat and wide roads. How much regret do they have? Is it true that there are tigers and wolves in the way, making people sigh with the difficulty of walking? However, the world is rugged, and thorns are everywhere. Where is there not a tiger's mouth? Alas...

Strange Stone 104

— Jiguan

Years ago, I studied in Beiping. During the summer vacation, I went with many friends to explore the scenery of Badaling. This place is connected to the Great Wall. Upon climbing it, I only saw the wind howling outside the fortress and the dust swirling. My heart was stirred. Stones are abundant in this area, often resembling the shapes of plants, trees, clouds, and smoke. My companions occasionally found some and regarded them as strange. I found one on the sand next to the wall, about half a foot in size. Upon closer inspection, it had pine branches on it, with several slender grasses nearby, as if carved. I placed it on my desk when I returned, but it was not considered strange. When I brought it south and showed it to my friend Mr. Cheng, Mr. Cheng said it was a fragment of the Great Wall's foundation stone. He knew its name from visiting the area north of the Kou Pass in the past. The stone had aged over the years and assimilated with the plants and trees. It could predict the weather. Its special characteristic was that whenever it was about to rain, the stone containing the branches and leaves would show a moist color. And when it was clear, the opposite would be true. Paying attention to testing it, I found that it matched. Therefore, I knew that the stone could also be treasured and used to predict the weather.

Recently, a friend, Mr. Gai, came from Dakou and gave me two stones in the shape of a square obstacle. I was surprised by the gift. Mr. Gai said that these stones came from Dakou and were rarely seen elsewhere. Because the swallows of the south fly across the Dakou River, and the chicks they hatch often fall to the bottom of the water. Over the years, they combine with the mud and soil, forming stones transformed from swallows. Local people dig on both sides of the river and often find them. Over the years, foreigners have come here to collect them. Those with a clear and elegant appearance are carved into squares and circles and decorated with frames, regarded as good products for embellishing studies and painting halls. However, those with vivid and picturesque scenes have been rare in recent years. These two stones each have traces of algae and duckweed, interspersed with small swallows, soaring and flying, with many different postures. They are naturally made, and so strange. One can't help but sigh at the craftsmanship of the creator. Our country is vast and rich in resources. The strangeness of stones is not limited to this. I only recorded what I collected to show a glimpse of it.

Letter to the Editor of Free Talk: I recently read a letter from WUB in your publication stating that the Cao Chef column in our newspaper's eighth volume, issue twenty-five supplement, was a reprint of UB's "Gossip from the Political Sea." The editor of this newspaper should be fully responsible for this matter. After investigation, the manuscript was submitted by "Luyang Kan Shang Sanren," whose real name is Yang Weibei, currently residing at No. 4, Miaojin Lane, Yangzhou. The editor of this newspaper has a limited understanding and failed to remember BU's great work, hence this small mistake. Now, he has been deceived of a "Guowen Weekly." Plagiarism of other people's work is an immoral act, and the responsibility lies where it belongs. Respectfully request that you disclose this to clarify the truth. Editorial Department of Guowen Weekly, 29th.

Memories of Escaping the Summer Heat at West Lake 105

— Yuan Rongfang

Bai Juyi wrote in his poem, "Unable to bear to leave Hangzhou, half of my lingering is for this lake." I have been living in Wulin for ten springs and autumns, but I have been bound by my work in the telecommunications business and have not had the leisure to fully enjoy the beauty of the lake and mountains, to emulate Bai Fu's leisurely wandering, poetry, wine, and laughter. It is not appropriate to compare them on the same day. Last summer, I painfully experienced the suffering of illness and felt that the scenery of the lake and mountains was full of sadness, so desolate that I could not bear to stay. This spring, I traveled to Shanghai, where the city was filled with bright lights and bustling crowds. The jade flutes and pearl hairpins were extremely prosperous and luxurious, just like the golden powder of the Southern Dynasties. But now, under the scorching sun, I feel tired and weary. I yearn for a cool place to spend half a day, hoping to refresh my mind. But I can't find one. Looking back at the beauty of the Six Bridges and the Three Temples, I am even more haunted by Li Bai's dream of Tianmu Mountain.

When the summer heat arrives, the people of Hangzhou always take pleasure in living in the mountains. Most of them stay in the monks' dormitories. At this time, the large temples on the lake, such as Lingyin, Tianzhu, Jingci, Yuquan, and Fenglin, are all full of guests. The other smaller temples are also filled with students. The climate in the mountains is cool, the temples are clean, the vegetarian dishes are exquisite, and the flowers, trees, and meditation rooms are suitable for escaping the summer heat.

Every summer, I would wake up between 3:00 AM and 5:00 AM. After washing up, I would go out of Hou Chao Gate in the waning moon and remaining stars. I would cross Wansong Ridge and arrive at the lake. The morning air and breeze in the mountains would bring a new coolness. The dew on the pine and willow trees would be dense, resembling pearls on my sleeves. The intermittent sounds of bells would echo each other. Sometimes I would go to Jingci Temple to watch the monks perform their morning prayers. The ancient Buddha, green lamps, red fish, and palm leaves created a peaceful and otherworldly atmosphere. Sometimes I would go to Su Causeway to watch the dawn. I would stroll on the Six Bridges. When it was sunny, thousands of rays of sunlight would shoot onto the blue waves, shining with gold and jade. When it was cloudy, the smoke and fog would cover the lake, and the clouds and mountains would appear and disappear, resembling Mi Fu's paintings. The wonderful scenery would change in an instant. Standing and staring, I would feel dizzy and entranced. Even if Wang Wei were resurrected, he would not be able to capture its beauty. When I had enough fun, I would either follow the shade of the willows along Su Causeway to Qiying or buy a small boat and enter Qingbo Gate to return. I would usually be back between 9:00 AM and 11:00 AM.

"Ultimately, the West Lake in June is different from the four seasons. The boundless green lotus leaves connect to the sky, and the lotus flowers reflected in the sun are especially red." This is a poem by a Song dynasty poet. It shows the value of West Lake in the summer during the Song dynasty. Now, times have changed, and the lotus leaves on the lake are no longer as prosperous as they used to be. When I first arrived in Hangzhou, there were still many plantings in the Houhu and Gushan areas. Whenever I had free time, I would often row a small boat through the Jin Dai Bridge in the faint morning light. I would row through the flowers. Even if the boat was not tied, there was no worry of being blown away. The golden light was everywhere, and the fragrance filled the lake. At that time, I would recite Cheng Zhai's poem "Early Morning Chant" and listen to the song of the lotus-picking girls of Yue. I would feel relaxed and carefree.

Novel-Reading Rotary Club

Woman, Woman (13) 106

— Yao Sufeng

Mr. Lu couldn't refuse any longer. Although he felt it wasn't appropriate to go to Suzhou, he thought it wouldn't be so coincidental that his family would see him. Besides, this was the best opportunity to make further advances with Miss Ding. So, he no longer objected and even hoped to leave sooner.

"So, when are we going?" he asked.

"We'll go tomorrow. We can play for two days," the young lady said.

After talking for a while, Miss Ding had to go home. Mr. Lu escorted her all the way to her house. They agreed to depart together from her home on the 5:05 PM express train the next day.

Reluctantly parting, Mr. Lu didn't feel like going back to the school dorm, so he stayed overnight at a hotel.

When Miss Ding returned home, her mother was still awake. Qiuzi had already told her everything she had seen, describing Mr. Lu as a beautiful fairy in a fairy tale and the scene in the reception room as a story of golden boys and jade girls. Mrs. Ding was very happy and wanted to wait for her daughter to come back and ask her about it in detail.

"Where have you been? Who did you go with?" Mrs. Ding asked her daughter with a mysterious smile.

"Mom! I was just about to tell you! Mom! Look, this ring was given to me by one of my classmates." She said shyly and haltingly.

"In today's world, old people like us really don't understand anything anymore. Unlike when we were young, such a thing would at least take a month or two, arranging a meeting, matching horoscopes, sending gifts. How can it be so easy now?" Mrs. Ding said, peering at the diamond ring on her daughter's hand, while smiling slightly.

Miss Ding was very shy and had nothing else to say, only silently fiddling with her belt.

Mrs. Ding continued, "So, what kind of person is that Mr. Lu?"

Miss Ding didn't say a word. She found it difficult to answer. Qiuzi, standing beside her, said with a smile, "Madam! That Mr. Lu and Miss are a match made in heaven!"

"What does his family do?" Mrs. Ding continued to ask.

"His father is a country gentleman from Suzhou. He owns a lot of land and property," Miss Ding replied softly.

"Good! Originally, this is your own business. If you are happy, that's all that matters. I only have one daughter like you. You can make all the decisions yourself!" Mrs. Ding smiled kindly.

It was very late, and Mrs. Ding went to bed. Miss Ding pretended to blame Qiuzi for being talkative, but in her heart, she felt much more comforted.

The night passed in sweet dreams. She felt a taste lingering in her heart that she had never experienced before. Even when she woke up, it seemed that a lingering passion was shaking her soul forever.

She got up and instructed Qiuzi to pack a few clothes and some toiletries in a small suitcase. She herself went to her mother and told her that she was going to Suzhou to play for two days.

Her mother loved her very much and naturally let her make her own decisions. She only instructed her, "Be careful on the road and come back after two days!"

From nine in the morning to four in the afternoon, Miss Ding felt that time was passing excessively slowly. It was not until Mr. Lu arrived that they went to the station together. They both had their own joy.

Continued Rise of Nine Taels in Value Yesterday, the 7th, the gold market continued to show a sharp and rapid rise in value, but the situation was peaceful. American Cotton Falls Below 8-fen Mark 116

American Cotton Continues to Fall, Indian and British Cotton Rebound: Yesterday, American cotton initially firmed due to good news from Liverpool, but later weakened due to estimates of favorable cotton harvests and good weather, with futures falling 2 to 5 pounds and spot goods falling 5 pounds. British cotton futures rose 3 points, and spot goods rose 5 points. Egyptian cotton spot goods rose 5 points. Indian cotton firmed due to better Liverpool market prices, with Pingguoer rising 2.75 rupees, Aomula rising 2.25 rupees, and Bailuoxi rising 2 rupees. Three Private Estimates of American Cotton 117

New York, 6th: The Memphis Commercial Appeal's estimate of the new cotton crop is 73.4% of the normal annual production, totaling 14,117,000 bales.

Gerber & Company estimates the new cotton crop at 71.0% of the normal annual production, totaling 13,730,000 bales. The previous estimate (July 7) was 41,986,000 mu of cotton fields.

The U.S. Cotton Crop Reporting Board estimates the new cotton crop at 70.6% of the normal annual production, totaling 13,456,000 bales. The previous estimate (July 6) was 74.2% of the normal annual production, totaling 12,400,000 to 13,400,000 bales, with 41,304,000 mu of cotton fields.

Grains: Hexia Rice Rises Again by Half a Yuan 118

Thick Medium-Grain Rice Is Again Being Stored on the Docks

And There Are Private Exports

South Market: The source of supply from various guilds is around the 12th to 14th. Due to scarce sales and movement from urban and rural shops, foreign rice has soared in price. In addition, Dongxin Medium-Grain Rice has increased by another half yuan and is also in short supply among the customers, which makes people feel more upward, and the intention to import is quite strong. Thick Medium-Grain Rice is slightly stored on the docks, and the situation is rapidly increasing by half yuan. Thin early rice is scarce, sales are very active, and the price has increased by three or four jiao. Foreign Lu Rice is high, short, and in demand, sharply increasing by three jiao. Zhongguan Rice sales are..., Yin Yuan Rice inventory is sporadic, and the exchange to Silver Yuan is difficult, sales are quite active, and the market is also tight. Foreign rice from Hankou guilds continues to be purchased, but the dock inventory is weak, and the market is increasing daily.

New Gate: Yesterday, a dozen or so supplies came from inland areas, and transactions on this street became more active. Each shop is taking advantage of this opportunity to add to its inventory, and people's hearts are tightening. A telegram from the West Road reported that the market for coarse medium-grain rice is upward, but this city is affected by it. It is learned that there are private exports, 500 shi of Changxi top medium-grain rice, and the price has risen by four or five jiao. Qingjiao thin early rice and Fenglian goods have each increased by five jiao. Lubu fine rice and foreign fine rice are purchased by customers, and the meager inventory is swept away, and the price has also increased by two jiao. There is a shortage of Yin Yuan Rice, and the price is tight.

Flour Market Enters a Stable Path 119

Yesterday, the flour market generally presented a stable path. Although the quoted price of foreign wheat fell again by two jiao, and Chicago fell to four jiao and seven fen, creating a record low not seen abroad, the domestic floods are also an unprecedented disaster, and the sound of disaster has stirred the ears and eyes of the whole country. Therefore, although factories are actively booking foreign wheat to maintain their future production, the Yangtze River guilds are also taking advantage of market to offset the losses of the floods. Therefore, this movement out and back in has created the conditions for a more stable market, otherwise the buyers and sellers would not be able to carry out their trades, and the market would not be so stable. Looking at the future, we should look at the real sales situation to see which way it goes. As a result, this month is 7.5 li better than the previous day, September is 5 li better, October/November is 1 fen better, December is 7.5 li better, and January is 5 li better.

Silk and Tea: Shandong Filature Silk Prices are High but No Transactions 120

Yesterday, the Shanghai filature silk market was silent. It was learned that Shandong Yellow Filature Silk this year has a poor cocoon production and the silk itself is not loose. Although there were negotiations in the market yesterday, Shandong silk merchants asked for 900 taels for their silk in hand, but the French buyers felt the price was too high and there were no transactions. American sales are still stagnant. Yesterday, only Weicheng Company bought 5 bales of Huaihu White Filature Silk, and Boxing bought 10 bales of Yellow Filature Silk, and the price remained firm.

Lüzhuang Green Tea is Firm 121

Yesterday, the Shanghai filature tea market saw strong interest from British and French buyers for Lüzhuang zhenmei, xiaomei, big-leaf fengmei, and xiumei green teas, as well as white-tipped teas. Fine zhenmei teas were particularly popular. Tea merchants, seeing that the market inventory was low and the supply exhausted, asked for higher prices, and the green tea market has reached a stable level. Qimen black tea saw slight interest from Yihua and Xintai yesterday, but because the market had been stagnant for a long time, the selling price was seen to fall by more than ten taels.

North-South Goods: Xiamen Candied Tangerines Are Scarce and Expected to Rise 122

There have been no deliveries of Xiamen candied tangerines in the previous two rounds, and the market inventory is low. It was learned that only 20 barrels were transported on the Huizhou ship, and the quoted price in the letter has risen, so the price on the market is tight again. Given the scarcity of supply, the asking price is bound to rise again, with an expected increase of about 8 qian, as Xiamen candied tangerine dough is soft and extremely suitable for customer needs.

Sugar Market Sees Raw and White Sugar Prices Blooming 123

Yesterday, the sugar market received telegrams from the producing areas: Cuban spot sugar prices remained unchanged, New York sugar futures rose two points in September and December, and rose one point in March of next year. There was no change in May. Java spot and futures sugar remained unchanged. The guild’s price list for Dutch No. 24 raw and white sugar was blooming, but transactions were very few. The asking price was 11 taels and 4 qian, and the market was firm. No. 20 medium white sugar was 10 taels, 8 qian, 7 fen and a half. No. 89 Dutch red sugar was 9 taels and 3 qian, and the trend was still good. Taikoo sugar imports and exports were quite strong: B: 11 taels and 9 qian, CW: 11 taels, 7 qian and a half to 7 qian and 7 fen and a half, DY: 11 taels and 7 qian and a half, HX: 11 taels and 6 qian, HM: 11 taels and 2 qian. The market was quite good. Huaxin listed 1,500 bags of B sugar at a price of 11 taels and 9 qian. Zhenxiang sold 9,902 bags of newly arrived raw white sugar at a price of 11 taels and 4 qian. Jinfat sold 1,000 bags at a price of 11 taels and 3 qian and a half. Buyers were very interested and all sold quickly, and the market was firm.

Local News

Wang Zhengting's Remarks 143

Jiang Zuobin to Assume Post in Japan Soon

Representatives to the League of Nations to be Selected Separately

Report on the Korean Incident to be Released Soon

Chen Youren to Return Home Soon

Coming to Shanghai to Mourn the Death of Madame Sun Yat-sen

Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting arrived in Shanghai by express train from Beijing at 11 o'clock last night. This newspaper’s reporter interviewed him in the train. According to Foreign Minister Wang, the newly appointed Ambassador to Japan, Jiang Zuobin, will assume his post in Japan in the shortest possible time. Because it is a tense period in Sino-Japanese diplomacy, the Ambassador to Japan has extremely important responsibilities and cannot delay for too long. As for the representatives to attend the League of Nations meeting, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will select other personnel and submit them to the National Government for appointment. The League of Nations meeting will open on September 7th, and it is feared that it will not be possible to rush there from the country, so it has been decided that the ambassador stationed abroad will serve concurrently. The candidates have not yet been decided. Ambassador Wang Rongbao has already met with him in Beijing. I have also read the written report of the Korean Incident investigation. I am instructing the department to organize it, and after it is organized, it will be published in the newspapers. The investigation report is a matter of fact and there is no need for secrecy. I came to Shanghai to mourn the death of Madame Sun Yat-sen. I am scheduled to pay my respects tomorrow (ie today). I will return to Beijing on Monday. As for the rumors that I will meet with Japanese Ambassador Shigemitsu Aoi in Shanghai tomorrow morning (ie today), the Ministry of Foreign Affairs did not make an appointment in advance. It is also unknown whether he will come to meet me temporarily. The reporter finally asked about Chen Youren's actions in Japan. What is the truth? Wang replied that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs had repeatedly received reports on Chen's mission to Japan, and the Japanese government also sent a statement to the Ministry. Chen knew very well that he could not do anything in Japan, and he will definitely return to China in the next day or two.

The Social Bureau Issued a Notice Yesterday

Promoting the Factory Law 144

Direct Action Not Allowed Against Violators

Reports Should be Submitted Before the End of This Month

The Factory Law and the Regulations for the Implementation of the Factory Law came into effect on August 1. In order to promote the implementation, the Shanghai Social Bureau issued a notice to all factory labor and management in the city yesterday: For the purpose of issuing a notice, if there are any factories in the city that have not fully complied with the law, the workers of the factory should report to the trade union and submit it to this bureau for review and handling. Direct action is not allowed to avoid disputes. In addition, all factories must submit all matters that should be reported in accordance with the provisions of the Factory Law to this bureau before the end of this month. It is hereby announced to all factory labor and management in this city to abide by it, and do not violate or neglect it.

Request a Thorough Investigation

The Theory of Extending the Concession 145

Unanimous Demand from All Circles in Western Shanghai

In the Puxong District of Western Shanghai, in areas such as Zhoujiaqiao, there were people posing as representatives of merchants and civilians who requested the Municipal Council to extend the concession, which has been detailed in previous reports. It is now learned that Gu Hongjun and Chen Zhenbai, citizens of Zhoujiaqiao in the district, and others have jointly submitted a request to the Municipal Committee, which will be forwarded to the Municipal Government, for a strict investigation. It is also learned that Chen Yafu, the Municipal Committee member of the district, immediately went to Zhoujiaqiao, Wangjialou, Chengjiaqiao and other places to conduct door-to-door investigations after reading the Da Mei Evening News the day before. According to the merchants and civilians in the area, there is indeed no such outrageous and traitorous act of willingly selling out the country. However, there is a reason for everything. The committee member has already obtained some clues and submitted them to the Municipal Government for strict investigation, and also requested that the truth be clarified to the Municipal Council. It is believed that the truth will not be difficult to reveal. The text of the submission is recorded below:

Submission from the Municipal Committee of Puxong District: Submitting a report on the matter of posing as a representative to request the Municipal Council to extend the concession, requesting review and thorough investigation based on the situation, and requesting clarification of the truth to the Municipal Council. According to the report from Gu Hongjun and other citizens of Zhoujiaqiao in the district, recently, the newspapers have reprinted reports saying, "200,000 merchants and civilians in Western Shanghai have jointly requested the Municipal Council to extend the concession, and purchase land to build police stations and collect police donations from shops, residents and factories along the roads, etc." After reading it, they were shocked. The citizens of Western Shanghai have always abided by their duties, and their patriotic concepts have never fallen behind others. In the past, due to the various relations of building roads beyond the boundary, they have been oppressed by imperialists for a long time, and they have endured it in silence for more than a day. Now, in the midst of the movement to recover the concession, unexpectedly, there is the absurd and outrageous thing of the so-called 200,000 merchants and civilians in Western Shanghai jointly requesting the Municipal Council to extend the concession. Moreover, it is not known who the 200,000 people are, and what qualifications they have to represent the name of the 200,000 people in Western Shanghai, so that the 200,000 people are all charged with the notoriety of selling out the country. And what methods did the Municipal Council use to obtain the written request of 200,000 people? For the sake of China's national rights and the future of the 200,000 citizens of Western Shanghai, we absolutely cannot recognize this kind of flattery of foreigners, profit-seeking, power-losing and country-humiliating behavior. Therefore, we specially submit a report to the committee for review, and request the Municipal Government to send a committee to conduct a strict investigation as soon as possible. What kind of treacherous slaves dare to pose as 200,000 merchants and civilians in Western Shanghai and commit this act of selling out the country? And ask the Municipal Council where the so-called written request of 200,000 people came from, and strictly arrest the national traitors who pose as traitors, and strictly investigate them to rectify the national law and eliminate the foreigners' ambitions to covet and attempt. The 200,000 citizens of Western Shanghai have been unjustly humiliated, or they can be exonerated. The situation is extremely urgent. According to this, after learning about the Da Mei Evening News, I immediately went to Zhoujiaqiao, Wangjialou, Chengjiaqiao and other places to conduct door-to-door investigations. They all said that in this season of singing loudly about recovering the concession, our merchants and civilians would never dare to do anything against their conscience unless they were insane. The report in the newspaper that the citizens requested the Municipal Council to extend the concession is completely fabricated. It is found that this act of posing as a representative and doing something outrageous is caused by treacherous people and local bullies causing trouble in order to flatter foreigners, or it is a groundless rumor created by the Municipal Council. According to the previous situation, it is reasonable to submit a report to your office for review and prompt investigation, and request that the Municipal Council clarify the truth to punish those who pose as representatives and extend the true public opinion. It is for the public good. Sincerely submit (omitted below)

Emergency Meeting of the Caojiadu Citizens' Association In Western Shanghai, the Third Branch of the Caojiadu Citizens' Association convened an emergency meeting at 8 pm the day before yesterday. More than 20 executive and standing committee members including Yao Yuguan, Chen Yunquan, Yu Yuqing, Zhu Rongping, Zhou Shangen, Zhu Heyun, Jin Fuchun, Li Meiqing, and Zhu Zhixian attended the meeting. First, the chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting, saying briefly, "On the 5th of this month, newspapers in this city reprinted the Da Mei Evening News's publication of 200,000 merchants and civilians in Zhoujiaqiao and other places in Western Shanghai jointly requesting the Public Concession Municipal Council to extend the Western Shanghai Concession. After reading it, we were deeply horrified. This area is adjacent to Zhoujiaqiao and other places, and we have never heard of it before. We are afraid that there may be misunderstandings from various parties, so we should urgently clarify the facts. Since the development of the market in this area over the years, the fire brigade was the first to be established, in the ninth year of the Republic of China. In the twelfth year, the Merchants and Civilians Association was established, and then the Defense Corps was established. This year, the association was reorganized. In the middle, due to the water relationship in the fire, conflicts have occurred with the concession many times. Members of the Defense Corps passed through the road and also negotiated with the Municipal Council before they were able to pass unobstructed. The addition of six district police stations, the expansion of posts, the recovery of police power, and the recovery of cleaning and hygiene, etc., are even more obvious to everyone. Moreover, for other matters involving national sovereignty and vital interests, we have assisted and requested the authorities to do their best to fight for them without any retreat. It can be seen that the patriotic enthusiasm of the citizens in this area has always been second to none. However, some people are willing to be accomplices and are still afraid that foreigners will not know how to progress, and even request the extension of the concession. Such flattery of foreigners, seeking personal gain, losing power and humiliating the country, and the ghostly tricks of shameless faces openly appear under the clear sky and bright sun. Isn't this a strange thing? The citizens of this area are a part of Western Shanghai, and they have sympathy for their anger. Moreover, the establishment of this association was originally to assist the party and government authorities to actively recover the roads built beyond the boundary and abolish unequal treaties. Therefore, we should investigate the truth, how to proceed with handling, please discuss and vote." After the committee members discussed for a long time and expressed their opinions one after another, it was decided to submit a report to the party and government organs and the Citizens' Association, requesting a strict investigation of the outrageous and falsely requested representatives, and requesting the Municipal Council to clarify the origin of the letter, and requesting the Municipal Government to quickly install water and electricity and repair the road surface on the roads built beyond the boundary in preparation for actively recovering the roads built beyond the boundary. The meeting was adjourned and the bell rang eleven times.

The 10th District Party Department Requests a Thorough Investigation The 10th District Party Department submitted a report to the Municipal Party Department yesterday regarding the reports in the newspapers that 200,000 people in Western Shanghai jointly requested the Municipal Council to extend the concession, requesting a thorough investigation. The exploration report is recorded below: Submitting a report for the matter of submission. Since the Da Mei Evening News disclosed the news that merchants and civilians in Western Shanghai requested the Municipal Council to extend the concession, all nationals have believed it to be true, and they have been angry and fearful, saying that the sovereignty of Western Shanghai is about to be lost. It is found that Zhoujiaqiao, Wangjialou, Chengjiaqiao and other places in Western Shanghai are within the scope of the headquarters of this district. They are all small town markets. If there are treacherous merchants living there and committing this act of selling out the country and flattering foreigners, the comrades of this association hate it even more. Since receiving the news, the committee members have been going to the places to inquire and investigate in detail. For example, in Zhoujiaqiao, there are Xinmin and Minsheng textile mills, which have become prosperous. Wangjialou has only a dozen small shops, and Chengjiaqiao has only seven or eight. After investigating each household and inquiring about the main partners, they all said that in recent years, the national spirit of our people has gradually increased, and the government is actively recovering the concession and the roads built beyond the boundary. The people should do their best to support the government. Although we were born in the market, we still know the great righteousness. How can we be insane and be accomplices and sell out the country for glory? According to yesterday's newspapers, one of the merchants' expressions has been ordered, which shows that there are no merchants in Western Shanghai who dare to commit this outrageous act. However, there must be a reason for the occurrence of an event. Although there is no such person among the merchants and civilians in Western Shanghai, there must be a reason for everything. There must be a reason for the generation of the driving force, and we should try to explore and find out the bottom line so that we can understand its content and plan for prevention and resistance. In the opinion of the comrades of this association, the reason is nothing more than two points: one is the behavior of local bullies, and the other is the coveting of foreigners. In the psychology of the bullies, they originally relied on the power of foreign merchants to sell the country to foreigners in order to make multiple profits. Now they see that the concession has become extremely developed and the land has become a fixed property for the industry owners. There are not many years to sell in and out, and there are fewer opportunities for them to make profits. Therefore, they have a whimsical idea and are willing to be accomplices and make this request to extend the concession in order to flatter the psychology of foreigners. If it is successful, they can follow it to return to their desire to make profits, and in a blink of an eye, they will become rich enough to boast of their assets. Even if it is not successful, it will not hurt them, or it can make foreigners happy, know their surnames, and then they can conspire and collude to sell the country and harm the people in order to fulfill their ambitions. There is no one more poisonous than this in the hearts of the scum of the country. Their coveting for foreigners is that at this time when our country is united to recover the concession and the campaign is the most intense, they are afraid that the truth will be difficult to hide and prevent the achievement of our country's recovery goal, so they borrow the mouths of merchants and civilians to conduct this counter-propaganda behavior in order to shake international hearing and create obstacles for our revenue. To maintain its concession life, its aggressive ambitions are fixed. Under this exaggerated atmosphere of rumors and extending the concession, we should first investigate whether there are any bullies who have requested, and the Municipal Council has made a large propaganda in the Da Mei Evening News, and its words must be based on something. We should request our government to make serious representations to it to clarify the truth. If the bullies really have such behavior, then quickly arrest them and bring them to justice to thank the people of the country. If it is caused by foreigners coveting, then we must pay attention to prevention, uphold justice, and publicize their aggressive ambitions to friendly countries, and actively carry out our work to achieve the goal of recovering the concession as soon as possible and restoring our sovereignty. We should ask the government and the people to work together to make a special report on the situation after the investigation to your association for review, one to express the feelings of the merchants and civilians in Western Shanghai, and one to request a thorough investigation of the origin of this statement, and to suspend the request for active handling to clarify the truth. The comrades of this association will do their best to follow behind to recover the concession. The country is fortunate. Sincerely submit. The association also received a report from more than 50 businesses including Liyuan in Zhoujiaqiao and more than 20 merchants and civilians including Gu Hongjun and Chen Zhen et al., requesting the transfer of the report to the Municipal Party Department, which has been transferred accordingly.

Serious Expression of the Citizens' Federation The Shanghai Special District Citizens' Federation telegraphed the National Government, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department, and the Shanghai Municipal Government for the recovery of the boundary-crossing roads that hinder sovereignty. The original Shanghai Public Concession was originally demarcated, but it was promoted due to the failure of the Qing Dynasty and the military阀 in power. The expansion of its scope is very different from the original boundary. The citizens of Shanghai deeply hate the foreigners' perversion and all attempt to recover it to rectify the national territory. However, due to the many events in the country and the environmental obstacles, it has not been successful. However, this aspiration has never been disregarded and we have always thought of freedom. Unexpectedly, foreigners' ambitions have not died and they have cleverly created rumors, wanting to promote it again. Its absurdity is ridiculous and hateful. It is found that the west of the Public Concession is limited to Jing'an Temple, but over the years, the Municipal Council has built roads beyond the boundary, advancing westward from the west end of Jing'an Temple, past Beixinjing and westward, naming its roads Yuyuan Road, Daxilu, Hualun Road, Lincoln Road, McLaughlen Road, Luobiegen Road, etc. No one who has a heart and has passed those roads can not be filled with anger. The association believes that at this time when negotiations to recover the concession have not yet matured, it is planned to first recover the roads built beyond the boundary, and immediately correct the names of the roads to rectify national rights and follow public opinion. I respectfully telegraph to you, please review and implement it. Yours sincerely, Shanghai Special District Citizens' Federation.

Record of the Anti-Japanese Propaganda Conference 148

More Than 1,000 People Attended the Meeting

The Shanghai Various Circles Anti-Japanese and Aid Overseas Chinese Committee held its first (Nanshi) Propaganda Conference at the Xiaoximen Juvenile Propaganda Group last night. About 1,000 people from all walks of life attended the meeting. Because the venue was small, it could not accommodate more people, so more than 100 people were restricted outside, which shows the people's indignation towards Japan. The grand occasion is recorded below:

Overview of the Venue Along the Zhonghua Road entrance, there were signs with the words "Shanghai Various Circles Anti-Japanese and Aid Overseas Chinese Propaganda Conference". The venue was full of slogans. The 250th Regiment of the Boy Scouts (East Asia Sports College) was in charge of discipline. The 65th Regiment (Business Union) played military music. There was a signing place at the entrance, and the Sino-French Pharmacy donated Rendan. The Nanyang Tobacco Company and Huacheng Tobacco Company donated cigarettes. Jiufutang donated paper fans, which showed their enthusiasm.

Conference Staff Chairman Xu Yefu, Recorder Hu Shuguang, Master of Ceremonies Song An, Reception Yao Ying, Guan Huaicong, Li Ruiying, Yu Zhongbiao, Affairs Tao Chengzhang, Zhou Xueying, Xu Huimin, Lv Zhongyuan.

Special Lecture First, the chairman reported on the significance of the meeting, and then invited Mr. Pan Zhan to give a lecture. In addition to briefly reporting on the Japanese killing of Korean overseas Chinese, he briefly said, "The Chinese people's anti-Japanese movement is not once, but each anti-Japanese time, Japanese imperialism insults us more once. The reason for this is that the Chinese people have not been able to oppose Japan permanently. Now the government is not the same as Yuan Shikai's government in the fourth year of the Republic of China, but is doing it in accordance with the Prime Minister's will. However, in the end, there are too many troublemakers in the country, such as the Red Bandits in Jiangxi, the abnormal situation in Guangdong, and the rebellion of the Shi Bandit in the north, which are too chaotic, so that the Japanese have the opportunity to invade. The so-called things must rot by themselves and insects will be born. At the same time, because of this relationship, the government's diplomacy is also difficult. At this time, our people should automatically oppose Japan, that is, vow not to sell Japanese goods, rely on everyone's conscience, and permanently economically cut off relations with Japanese imperialism, and be the backing of the government. As for unnecessary and boring reckless actions, for the sake of prudence, it should be avoided." The listeners were all moved.

Then, the gentlemen of the costume lecture group of the Juvenile Propaganda Group gave a lecture on "Who is the enemy?" Mr. Yao Mingxin and Feng Danbai performed a cross-talk show, which was extremely precise and vigilant.

News from the Meeting This conference was held in the hot summer, and there were more than a thousand listeners, which made the downstairs of the venue very crowded and could not accommodate any more people. About two hundred people could not enter the venue. Fortunately, the Boy Scouts and police officers explained politely, and the order was still good. However, the association expressed its apologies. Also, the association will hold its second propaganda conference next Sunday, and has specially hired Mr. Chen Binhe, a famous expert on Japan, to give an academic lecture. The venue will be in the Youth Association.

Australian Aviator Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday 151

Solo Flight from Australia to England

Arrived Safely at Songkou and Landed Yesterday Afternoon

Australian aviator Chi Qian Sde, driving a light plane, the "Ereca", flew from Taiwan to the Jiangmian River in Wusongkou at 4:20 pm yesterday and landed safely. He immediately added gasoline and was towed by a steamer to the Yangjinggang Jiangmian River opposite Yangshupu to stay overnight. Those who welcomed him on the Jianggan River were representatives of the British Royal Aviation Association and the Yinshike Association. Last night, the two groups held a banquet to welcome him. If the weather is good today, Mr. Chi Qian Sde will leave Shanghai at 7-8 am this morning and fly to Korea. Mr. Chi Qian Sde is a famous Australian aviator who looks very similar to Lenin. He once flew alone in the "Ereca" small plane to travel to England and Australia two years ago and achieved his flying goal in eighteen days. He is now still driving the original plane to make a solo flight from Australia via the Far East to London. He flew from Manila to Shanghai this Monday, first to the northernmost port of the Philippines, Cabali, and then to Taiwan. He originally hoped to arrive in Shanghai on Wednesday or Thursday, but later the plane landed in Taiwan and suffered minor damage, which led to the delay. He did not leave Taiwan until 9:45 am yesterday and flew 600 miles to Shanghai. After that, he will fly to Korea and Japan, then across the Pacific Ocean, across the Americas, and to London.

The Aviator Chi Qian Sde 152

News of Flood Relief in Various Provinces 153

Telegram Seeking Disaster Relief Funds: The Shanghai Emergency Relief Association for Flood Victims in Various Provinces held its inaugural meeting at the City Chamber of Commerce the night before last. Mr. Xu Jingren, Chairman of the Relief Committee, nominated Yu Hede, Wang Xiaolai, and Wang Zhen as temporary chairmen to jointly organize the association's affairs. Yesterday afternoon, Yu, Wang, and Wang invited Xu Jingren, Huang Hanzhi, Wen Lanting, Wu Zhihao, and Zhang Gongquan (representing Jin Houcheng) for a public meeting. During the meeting, it was decided that the number of executive committee members would be unlimited, but there would be eleven standing committee members and three secretaries-general to jointly handle the association's affairs. Internal affairs would still be handled by Mr. Jin Guanfu of the Relief Committee, along with the original staff. It was also decided that the first standing committee meeting would be held at 4:00 PM today. Subsequently, it was decided to send a telegram to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, stating that the people's donations were limited and requesting that he quickly allocate 20 million yuan in cash to handle emergency relief in various provinces. The original telegram is recorded below: "To His Excellency Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the Nanchang General Headquarters: Since the beginning of summer this year, continuous torrential rains have caused widespread flooding, affecting sixteen provinces and eighty million people. This unprecedented disaster has not been seen in a century. The Republic prioritizes the people's livelihood, but now tens of millions of flood victims are suffering from drowning and starvation, unable to guarantee their lives from morning till night. If we rely solely on the public to leisurely solicit donations, no matter how hard we try, the amount obtained will be limited and too slow to address the emergency. The dead are gone, and the living, especially the old and weak, will end up in ditches, while the strong will become bandits. Hede and others feel deeply concerned and dare to earnestly request Your Excellency, with a heart that feels the hunger and drowning of others as your own, to provide salvation and fulfill the government's duty. Immediately order the allocation of 20 million yuan in cash to expedite emergency relief in various provinces. This is an urgent plea, and we await your command with utmost trepidation. Respectfully, the Standing Committee Members of the Shanghai Emergency Relief Association for Flood Victims in Various Provinces, Yu Hede, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Zhen, Xu Shiying, Zhang Zhijiang, Huang Qinglan, Li Jin, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Lin Kanghou, Qin Runqing, bow in unison, Yang."

Relief Association Requests Funds: Mr. Xu Jingren, Chairman of the Relief Committee, is extremely concerned about the recent floods in various provinces. In addition to sending a telegram to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek requesting a large sum of money for relief, he has repeatedly appealed to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance for funds. The day before yesterday, Mr. Xu paid a special visit to Finance Minister Song Ziwen but was unable to meet him due to illness. Yesterday, he accompanied Mr. Wang Yiting, a member of the association's standing committee, to visit Mr. Zhang Yongni, the Deputy Minister of Finance. Mr. Zhang received them and promised to do his best to raise funds, informing them that Minister Song had agreed to first issue 2 million yuan in salt tax treasury bills, which could be collected on Tuesday of next week, to assist with emergency relief in various provinces. Once he recovers from his illness, he will return to the capital and submit disaster relief and rehabilitation measures to the State Council, issuing 20 million yuan in disaster relief bonds so that the major disasters in various provinces can be alleviated as much as possible. Mr. Xu and Mr. Wang expressed their deep gratitude to Mr. Song for his compassion and to Mr. Zhang for his enthusiasm on behalf of the flood victims. They also sent a telegram to the association in Nanjing, scheduling a relief meeting for the fourteenth to discuss emergency relief measures.

Jiangning Compatriots to Meet Tomorrow: The capital has been severely flooded this time, and the National Government has allocated funds to the Ministry of Interior to jointly establish an emergency relief association for the capital's flood, and expedites relief. However, the scope of the relief is limited to the capital city and its immediate suburbs, while the disaster-stricken area of the entire county is vast, making it difficult to reach everyone. Leng Jun, the Magistrate of Jiangning County, came to Shanghai on the fourth to discuss fundraising with prominent Jiangning figures such as Shi Liangcai, Sun Yuesan, Ha Shaofu, Xia Yizhai, Jin Guanfu, and Li Qin. However, this flood has affected not only Jiangning County but also all six counties formerly under Jiangning's jurisdiction. It is reported that the Jiangning Six Counties Association in Shanghai, the Jiangning Six Counties Public Office, and others will jointly launch the Jiangning Six Counties Flood Relief Association in Shanghai to raise relief funds. A notice has been issued inviting fellow villagers from the six counties to gather at the Jiangning Public Office on the ninth of this month to discuss the procedures.

Disaster Reports from Various Counties in Northern and Southern Anhui: The Anhui Fellow-Provincials Association yesterday received subsequent reports from five counties: Fengtai, Yingshang, Dingyuan, Hefei, and Xuancheng, recorded below: (1) Fengtai County: This summer's harvest was poor, causing concerns about food shortages. Since May, the Huai, Ying, and Fei rivers have overflowed, with black sludge swirling and blocking the county seat. The water level is several feet higher than any recorded in the past three hundred years. The disaster is particularly severe compared to neighboring areas. All 500,000 people in the county have lost their homes and property, with no food or shelter. They are scattered and displaced, with cries echoing to the heavens. Even if they escape being eaten by fish, they can only endure starvation in the mountains. Some, worried about the future, tie their families together and drown. Those who escape have no way to climb trees for food. Fields and houses have been washed away, and livestock are lost. Only the sound of waves is heard, with no cooking smoke to be seen. Looking out from a high place, the sight is heartbreaking. The continuous rain and increasing flood season worsen the disaster, with no end in sight. If emergency relief is not provided, there will be widespread starvation. (2) Yingshang County: Situated near the Huai and Sha rivers, the terrain is low and prone to flooding. Last year's autumn rains flooded the crops on both banks of the Sha and Huai rivers, leaving the farmers in each area almost completely empty-handed. This year's spring floods caused the wheat to fail, with no means of sustenance and no way to borrow money. They had hoped for a good autumn harvest, but Heaven did not spare them, and floods followed. The dikes were breached, and the entire area became a vast expanse of water, covering over 300 li and turning into a swamp. People and livestock were swept away, and houses were washed away. Grain and firewood were lost in the waves. Over 370,000 mu of land in the county were flooded, and over 20,000 houses collapsed. Those not yet destroyed can be heard groaning in the water. The drowned and starved cannot be buried. The living have no place to stay and cannot guarantee their lives. Currently, one dou of rice costs 13 strings of cash, one dou of wheat costs 9 strings of cash, and one dou of mung beans costs 16 strings of cash. Grain and firewood are cut off, and the future is bleak. (3) Dingyuan County: Mountain floods erupted, with turbulent waves sweeping down like an avalanche. Houses collapsed and were carried away by the water. New and old coffins were washed up. Livestock and people drowned in large numbers. Those who managed to escape were emaciated and awaiting rescue. They were exposed to the wind and dew, and the fields were destroyed, making it difficult to expect an autumn harvest. What will they eat this winter and next spring? (4) Xuancheng County: From the Zhen to the Yan days of this month, there were continuous rains for ten days, and the floods spread hundreds of li, turning the entire area into a vast swamp. All 200-plus embankments in the county collapsed, with countless fields and houses washed away, and people and livestock drowned. The dead cannot be found, and the living cannot be saved. Hundreds of thousands of victims have no clothes or food. The disaster area is too large to navigate with even a small reed boat. The pitiful survivors will fill the ditches. (5) Hefei County: On the Geng day, mountain floods erupted, and the county seat became a swamp. All the embankments were breached, and the fields and houses were washed away, with countless people and livestock dying. Such a catastrophic disaster is rare in a century. (6) A part of the Shou County city wall was washed away some days ago, and the floodwater poured into the city, drowning many people and livestock. Telegraph poles were destroyed, causing delays in mail and making the news very bad. The Anhui Guangji Embankment covers 200 li and has a population of over 300,000, serving as the lifeline for the food supply of seven counties including Tonghuai. Thirty years after being repaired following a collapse in the twenty-seventh year of the Guangxu reign (Qing dynasty), it collapsed again at the Qianjiangkou on the You day of July, flooding hundreds of li. Fields and houses were submerged, and people and livestock drifted away. The farmers' livelihood for the entire year was ruined, leaving the victims in groups, with mournful cries echoing across the fields, causing distress and sorrow. Since the day of the disaster, the Anhui Charity Joint Association, the Chamber of Commerce, and the Charity Society have been distributing 60 million jin of dry food in shifts. However, there are too many victims and limited charitable funds. Therefore, they have requested assistance from government authorities and have sent representatives, Mr. Wang Duqi to Shanghai and Mr. Fu Shunsheng stationed in Shanghai, to appeal for donations from all parties on behalf of the victims. It is reported that there have been some results. Citizens Zhao Shaofu, Zhang Yunbo, Lu Gongren, Sun Huanchen, Zhu Shaoting, Liu Xihan, Deng Yuntai, Chen Junsheng, etc., of Fengyang County, presented a public letter to Chairman Xu of the Relief Committee, requesting the allocation of funds for relief, describing the terrible conditions of the flood disaster in their county. The letter stated: "We present this letter to request assistance for the hungry and drowning due to the unprecedented disaster caused by continuous heavy rain and the convergence of rivers. Since mid-June to the end of July, there has been continuous heavy rain in the Huai River region. The river water was already high, and the Yellow River took advantage of this continuous rain to shift south, drawing the Wo and Ying rivers west and converging with the Yi and Si rivers east, joining the Huai River simultaneously. This vast expanse covers over ten counties and exceeds 2,000 li. Based on surveys, the rainfall exceeds the average by more than 400%. Not only are the dikes completely broken, and half the population and livestock have not escaped, but most of the villages on the water have been wiped out. What is even more tragic is that people climb trees to be rescued, and countless corpses float on the waves every day. Such a catastrophe is causing sorrow for heaven and earth. The book says 'embracing the mountains and encircling the hills,' but this is even worse. We citizens grew up on the Huai River and have accurate knowledge of the situation. The floods are as described above. Fengyang is located in the middle of the Huai River. Every time there is a major flood, the four bays of Zhu, Wei, Tang, and Yao in the east reach Linhuai and converge with the Beng River, spanning 70 li in a straight line from east to west and 50 li across the north and south banks. The area of this year's flood is undoubtedly more than twice that. The disaster situation in the upper reaches is even more severe. The water in the northwest of the county connects, and the northeast mixes and flows with the Huai and Ling rivers, and the lower reaches with the Si River, creating a vast expanse of water. Seven of the ten districts in the county have been flooded. The water level in Honghu Lake is higher than the Huai River, and the Yangtze River is also rising, making it difficult to expect a smooth discharge. Currently, agricultural tools are floating, and crops are being swept away by the waves. Alas, the people are dying of starvation, and half are displaced. If this continues for two months, it will be even worse. Only 30% of the fields in the county have not been flooded. Even if there is a harvest, it will only be enough to feed a quarter of the county's population. If we do not receive assistance, these small people, without fields or food, will undoubtedly fill the ditches. At this time of desperation, we dare to hope for a glimmer of hope. Fortunately, gentry in each district are preparing for emergency relief and carrying out rescues, but the funds are scarce and the efforts are weak. The districts that have not been affected by the disaster have experienced continuous heavy rain, with walls collapsing, houses collapsing, and firewood and grain depleted. Most of these families have relatives and friends, and it is difficult to expect them to provide assistance at all times. We urgently need widespread relief to avoid the deaths of many. We have long admired Mr. Chairman for his concern for the people and his extreme admiration for Yu and Ji. We are willing to sincerely report the unusual disaster in Anhui and the disaster situation in Fengyang to your seat for review and approval, and we earnestly request a thorough investigation to allocate relief funds fairly. The merits of this will be immeasurable."

Sichuanese Request Disaster Relief Bonds: The Sichuanese Association in Shanghai and the Sichuanese Anti-Rehabilitation Bonds Appeal Group, etc., believe that the drought in Sichuan Province is extremely severe, and the floods have also affected the southern, eastern, and northern parts of Sichuan, with over one million famine victims. The Sichuan Provincial Government previously requested the Central Government to issue 1 million yuan in disaster relief bonds, but the Ministry of Finance replied that it would "temporarily postpone discussion" and failed to approve it. However, Liu Xiang's request to issue 20 million yuan in rehabilitation bonds was readily approved. It seems that the Central Government is not fully aware of the situation in Sichuan. They plan to jointly send a telegram to the Central Government, expressing their concern for the disaster in Sichuan, withdrawing the order to issue rehabilitation bonds to alleviate the people's suffering. If it is necessary to issue bonds, they request that they be transferred to disaster relief bonds to save the disaster victims. The telegram is being drafted and will be sent out soon.

Citywide Boy Scouts to Hold Large-Scale Fundraising: The No. 383 Guanghua High School Troop, the No. 121 Southeast Girls' Physical Education School Troop, the No. 196 Liangjiang Girls' Physical Education School Troop, and the No. 268 Fudan High School Troop of the Shanghai Boy Scouts, recognizing the unprecedented disaster of floods in various provinces, and witnessing the plight of compatriots in the disaster areas who are unable to live or die, and hearing their heart-wrenching cries, based on the Boy Scouts' principle of doing one good deed every day, and the spirit of helping others at all times and in all places, have proposed to the Shanghai Boy Scouts Council to quickly organize a citywide Boy Scouts fundraising disaster relief association. The original report of the four troops is recorded below: "Report Regarding Requesting Fundraising for Disaster Relief to Assist a Righteous Cause, Requesting Review and Implementation. Since the beginning of the year, there has been continuous rain, and mountain floods have erupted, causing floods in more than a dozen provinces, affecting no less than 50 million people nationwide. Such a catastrophe is rare in nearly a century. The dead are drifting away without a trace, and the living are displaced. The disaster is severe and heartbreaking. We, the Boy Scouts, embrace benevolence and courage, and make knowledge and action our nature. We should take responsibility for providing relief in this major disaster. Recognizing this, the troops have jointly requested that the Council organize a citywide Boy Scouts fundraising disaster relief association to gather donations widely, hoping to accumulate a little to make a lot, and for everyone to work together to make things easy. Is this appropriate? We hereby submit this report to the Council for review and approval. It will be a great kindness."

Exemption of Business Tax for State-Owned Goods Commercial Field 156

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, in order to promote the sales of state-owned goods, recruited factories and shops to transform the entire first floor of the original Commodity Exhibition Hall into a State-Owned Goods Commercial Field, specializing in the sale of products from state-owned enterprises.
